

\subsubsection[The Westminster Larger Catechism of 1648]{{The Westminster Larger Catechism of
1648}}
Q. 1. \textit{What is the }chief\index{Mankind:chief end/purpose ``f10!}\textit{ and highest end of man?}

A. Man's chief\index{Mankind:chief end/purpose ``f10!} and highest end is to glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God
``f10!} God,\footnote{\ Romans 11:36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:31\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} and fully to enjoy him forever.\footnote{\ Psalm 73:24-28\index{19
Psalms:ch.  73, v.  24-28, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 2 \textit{How does it appear that there is a God?}

A. The very light of nature in man, and the works of God\index{Providence:God's works ``f10!}, declare
plainly\index{Revelation:natural:declares there is a God ``f10!} that there is a God;\footnote{\ Romans
1:19-20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 19:1-3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!};
Acts 17:28\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} but his word and Spirit\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit
``f10!} only do sufficiently and\index{Revelation:natural:not sufficient for salvation ``f10!} effectually
reveal\index{God's law:commandments:first revelation ``f10!} him unto men for their salvation\index{Salvation:belief in
Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 2:9-10\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15-17, pg. ``f30!};
Isaiah 59:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 3 \textit{What is the word of God?}

A. The holy\index{Scripture:holy ``f10!} scriptures of\index{Scripture:word of God:revelation ``f10!} the Old and New
Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}s are the word of God,\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 3:16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch. 
3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Peter 1:19\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   1, v. 
19-21, pg. ``f30!}.} the only rule of faith\index{Faith:rule of ``f10!} and obedience\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}0\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:18-19\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  18-19,
pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 8:20\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   8, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 16:29, 31\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v.  29,
31, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 1:8-9\index{48 Galatians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2
Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 4 \textit{How does it appear that the scriptures are}\index{Scripture:word of God:revelation ``f10!}\textit{ the word
of God?}

A. The scriptures manifest the\index{Providence:manifests goodness of God ``f10!}mselves to\index{Scripture:manifested
as word of God ``f10!} be the word of God, by their majesty\footnote{\ Hosea 8:12\index{28 Hosea:ch.   8, v.  12, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:6-7, 13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.   6-7, 13, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:18\index{19
Psalms:ch. 119, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}, 129\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  18, 129, pg. ``f30!}.} and
purity\index{Scripture:purity of ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm 12:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  12, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
119:140\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v. 140, pg. ``f30!}.} by the consent of all\index{Scripture:consent of all parts
``f10!} the parts,\footnote{\ Acts 10:43\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 26:22\index{44 Acts:ch.  26,
v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} and the scope of the whole, which is to give all glory\index{Scripture:gives glory to God ``f10!}
to God;\footnote{\ Romans 3:19, 27\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  19, 27, pg. ``f30!}.} by their light and
power\index{Scripture:light and power to convict sinners ``f10!} to convince and\index{Scripture:power to convince and
convert ``f10!} convert sinners\index{Conversion:conversion ``f10!}, to comfort\index{Scripture:comforts and builds up
believers ``f10!} and build up believers\index{Holy Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!} unto
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Acts 23:28\index{44 Acts:ch.  23, v.  28, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 4:12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:18\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 19:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 15:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:32\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.} but
the Spirit of God\index{Holy Spirit:God's Spirit ``f10!} bearing witness by\index{Scripture:witness to heart of man
``f10!} and with the scriptures in the heart of man, is alone able fully to persuade it\index{Scripture:Holy Spirit
persuades us that it is word of God ``f10!} that they are the very word of God.\footnote{\ John 16:13-14\index{43
John:ch.  16, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; John 20:31\index{43 John:ch.  20, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:2\index{62 1
John:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0, 27\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  20, 27, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 5 \textit{What do the scriptures principally}\index{Scripture:principal teaching ``f10!}\textit{ teach?}

A. The scriptures principally\index{Scripture:principal teaching ``f10!} teach, what man is to believe concerning God,
and what duty God\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} requires of man.\footnote{\ 2 Timothy
1:13\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 6 \textit{What do the scriptures make}\index{Scripture:makes God known ``f10!}\textit{ known of God?}

A. The scriptures make\index{Scripture:makes God known ``f10!} known what God is,\footnote{\ Hebrews 11:6\index{58
Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} the persons in the Godhead\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1
John 5:7\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} his decrees\index{Predestination:eternal decrees
``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 15:14-15, 18\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  14-15, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} and the execution of his
decrees.\footnote{\ Acts 4:27-28\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 7 \textit{What is God?}

A. God is a\index{God's attributes:listed (definition of God) ``f10!} Spirit,\footnote{\ John 4:24\index{43 John:ch.  
4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} in and of himself infinite in\index{God's attributes:infinite:in being ``f10!}
being,\footnote{\ Exodus 3:14\index{02 Exodus:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Job 11:7-9\index{18 Job:ch.  11, v.   7-9,
pg. ``f30!}.} glory,\footnote{\ Acts 7:2\index{44 Acts:ch.   7, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} blessedness,\index{God's
attributes:perfect blessedness ``f10!}\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and perfection;\footnote{\ Matthew 5:48\index{40 Matthew:ch.
5, v.  48, pg. ``f30!}.} all-sufficient\index{God's attributes:all-sufficient ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis
17:1\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} eternal,\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm
90:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  90, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} unchangeable\index{God's attributes:unchangeable
``f10!},\footnote{\ Malachi 3:6\index{39 Malachi:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:17\index{59 James:ch.   1, v. 
17, pg. ``f30!}.} incomprehensible\index{God's attributes:incomprehensible ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Kings 8:27\index{11 1
Kings:ch.   8, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} everywhere present\index{God's attributes:everywhere present
``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 139:1-13\index{19 Psalms:ch. 139, v.   1-13, pg. ``f30!}.} almighty\index{God's
attributes:almighty power ``f10!},\footnote{\ Revelation 4:8\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} knowing
all\index{God's attributes:omniscience ``f10!} things,\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 147:5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 147, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} most wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom
``f10!},\footnote{\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg.
``f30!} most
holy\index{God's attributes:holy:most ``f10!},\footnote{\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   6,
v.   3, pg. ``f30!}\index{66 Revelation:ch.  15, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.  32, v.   4, pg. ``f30!} most merciful\index{God's attributes:merciful
``f10!} and gracious\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}, long-suffering\index{God's attributes:long-suffering ``f10!}, and
abundant in goodness\index{God's attributes:goodness ``f10!} and truth\index{God's attributes:truth
``f10!}.\footnote{\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}


\bigskip

Q. 8 \textit{Are there more Gods than one?}

A. There is but one only, the living and true God.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:4\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 8:4, 6\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   4, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 10:10\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 9 \textit{How many persons}\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!}\textit{ are there in the
Godhead}\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. There be three persons\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!} in the Godhead\index{God's
attributes:Godhead ``f10!}, the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and the
Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}; and these three are one true, eternal God\index{God's
attributes:eternal ``f10!}, the same in substance\index{God's attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!}, equal in power
and glory\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!}; although distinguished\index{God's
attributes:trinity:distinguished by personal properties ``f10!} by their personal properties.\footnote{\ 1 John
5:7\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 3:16-17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 13:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}4\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:30\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  30, pg.
``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 10 \textit{What are the personal properties of}\index{God's attributes:trinity:distinguished by personal properties
``f10!}\textit{ the three persons}\index{God's attributes:trinity:three persons ``f10!}\textit{ in the
Godhead}\index{God's attributes:Godhead ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. It is proper to the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!} to beget\index{Jesus:begotten by the Father ``f10!} the
Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:5-6, 8\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   5-6, 8, pg. ``f30!}.}
and to the Son to be begotten of the Father,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43
John:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 18\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, 18, pg. ``f30!}.} and to the Holy Ghost\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!} to proceed from the\index{Holy Spirit:procession from Father and Son ``f10!} Father and the
Son from all eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 15:26\index{43 John:ch.  15, v.  26, pg.
``f30!}; Galatians 4:6\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 11 \textit{How does it appear that the Son}\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}\textit{ and the Holy Ghost}\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}\textit{ are God equal with the}\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!}\textit{
Father}\index{Father:God the ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The scriptures manifest that\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!} the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God
``f10!} and the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!} are God equal with the Father\index{Father:God the
``f10!}, ascribing unto\index{Worship:praising God's names ``f10!} them such names,\footnote{\ Isaiah 6:3\index{23
Isaiah:ch.   6, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}, 5, 8\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   6, v.   3, 5, 8, pg. ``f30!}; John 12:41\index{43
John:ch.  12, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 5:3\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.  
3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 28:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  28, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:20\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  20,
pg. ``f30!}.} attributes\index{God's attributes:to be:revered ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}; John 2:24-25\index{43 John:ch.   2, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 9:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.   6,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:10-11\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.}
works,\footnote{\ Colossians 1:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.  
1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} and worship,\index{Worship:acceptable manner ``f10!}\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40
Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 13:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{47
2 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} as are proper to God only.


\bigskip

Q. 12 \textit{What are the decrees}\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}\textit{ of God?}

A. God's decrees are\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} the wise\index{God's attributes:wisdom ``f10!}, free,
and holy acts\index{God's attributes:holy:acts ``f10!} of the counsel of his\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!}
will,\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 9:14-15, 18\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  14-15, 18, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11,
v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby, from all eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!}, he has, for his own
glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, unchangeably foreordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination
``f10!}: Whatsoever comes to pass in time,\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!},
11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, 11, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:22-23\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 33:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  33, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} especially concerning angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and
men.


\bigskip

Q. 13 \textit{What has God especially decreed}\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}\textit{ concerning
angels}\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}\textit{ and men?}

A. God, by an eternal and immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees
``f10!}, out of his mere love, for\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!} the praise of his glorious
grace\index{Grace:glorious ``f10!}, to be manifested\index{Grace:manifested ``f10!} in due time, has
elected\index{Election:some angels ``f10!} some angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} to glory\index{Angels:elected to
glory ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 5:21\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and in Christ has
chosen\index{Election:chosen by God ``f10!} some men to eternal life\index{eternal life ``f10!}, and the means
thereof:\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  
4-6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:13\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{53 2
Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} and also, according to his sovereign\index{God's attributes:sovereign
lordship ``f10!} power, and the unsearchable\index{Providence:unsearchable wise counsel ``f10!} counsel of
his\index{Causation:God's own will ``f10!} own will (whereby he extends or withholds\index{Providence:God withholds
mercy, grace, favour as he wills ``f10!} favor as\index{Predestination:God's favour as he pleases ``f10!} he
pleases\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!}), has passed by and
foreordained\index{Predestination:fore-ordination ``f10!} the rest to dishonor and\index{Resurrection:wicked raised in
dishonour ``f10!} wrath, to be\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!} for their sin
inflicted\index{Predestination:mankind:unto reprobation ``f10!}, to the praise of the\index{Worship:praising God
``f10!} glory of his justice\index{God's attributes:administers justice ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 9:17\index{45
Romans:ch.   9, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18, 21-22\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  17-18, 21-22, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
11:25-26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11, v.  25-26, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 2:2\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}0\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 1:4\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter
2:8\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 14 \textit{How does God execute his decrees}\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. God executes his decrees\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} in the works of creation\index{God's
attributes:creator:works of ``f10!} and providence\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}, according to his
infallible\index{God's attributes:infallible fore-knowledge ``f10!} foreknowledge\index{God's attributes:foreknowledge
``f10!}, and the free and immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!} counsel of his\index{Causation:God's own
will ``f10!} own will.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.
1, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 15 \textit{What is the work of creation}\index{God's attributes:creator:works of ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The work of creation\index{God's attributes:creator:works of ``f10!} is that wherein God did in the beginning, by the
word of his power\index{Creation:by word of God's power ``f10!}, make of nothing the world, and all things therein, for
himself, within the space of six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days, and all very good.\footnote{\ Genesis 1;
Hebrews 11:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 16:4\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  16, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}.} 


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 16 \textit{How did God create angels}\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. God created all the angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}\footnote{\ Colossians 1:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v. 
16, pg. ``f30!}.} spirits,\footnote{\ Psalm 104:4\index{19 Psalms:ch. 104, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}
immortal,\footnote{\ Matthew 22:30\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} holy,\footnote{\ Matthew
25:31\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} excelling in knowledge\index{Angels:attributes
``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Samuel 14:17\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  14, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 24:36\index{40 Matthew:ch. 
24, v.  36, pg. ``f30!}.} mighty in power,\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 1:7\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   7, pg.
``f30!}.} to execute his\index{Angels:created to execute God's commands ``f10!} commandments, and to praise
his\index{Worship:praising God ``f10!} name,\footnote{\ Psalm 103:20-21\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.  20-21, pg.
``f30!}.} yet subject to change.\footnote{\ 2 Peter 2:4\index{61 2 Peter:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 17 \textit{How did God create man}\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. After God\index{Mankind:created:attributes ``f10!} had made all other creatures\index{creatures ``f10!}, he created
man\index{Mankind:created:by God ``f10!} male\index{Mankind:male and female ``f10!} and
female\index{Mankind:created:male and female ``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} formed the body of the man of the dust\index{Adam:formed of
dust ``f10!} of the ground,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} and the woman of the
rib\index{Eve, from Adam's rib ``f10!} of the man,\footnote{\ Genesis 2:22\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}.} endued the\index{Causation:will of creatures:natural liberty ``f10!}m with living,
reasonable\index{Mankind:created:reasonable soul ``f10!}, and immortal\index{Mankind:immortal soul ``f10!}
souls;\footnote{\ Genesis 2:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Job 35:11\index{18 Job:ch.  35, v.  11,
pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes 12:7\index{21 Ecclesiastes:ch.  12, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 10:28\index{40 Matthew:ch. 
10, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 23:43\index{42 Luke:ch.  23, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}.} made them after his own
image\index{Mankind:image of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}7\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} in knowledge,\footnote{\ Colossians 3:10\index{51

``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:24\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} having the law of God written in

``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}.} and power to fulfil it\index{Covenant:works:conditional

Ecclesiastes:ch.   7, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} and dominion over the\index{Mankind:dominion over creation ``f10!}

``f30!}.} yet subject to fall.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ecclesiastes

Q. 20 \textit{What was the providence}\index{Providence:providence ``f10!}\textit{ of God toward man in the estate

``f10!}\textit{?}

``f30!}.} and ordaining\index{Marriage:ordained by God ``f10!} marriage for his help\index{Marriage:mutual help
``f10!};\footnote{\ Genesis 2:18\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} affording him communion with

Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-29\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v. 
26-29, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 3:8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} instituting\index{Sabbath:instituted by

obedience ``f10!} of personal, perfect, and perpetual obedience\index{Covenant:works:perpetual obedience required
``f10!},\footnote{\ Galatians 3:12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch. 
10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} of which the tree of life\index{Tree:of life, pledge to first covenant ``f10!} was a

pg. ``f30!}.} and forbidding\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!} to eat of the tree of the\index{Tree:of

Q. 21 \textit{Did man continue in that estate}\index{Mankind:created:state of innocence ``f10!}\textit{ wherein God at

A. Our first parents\index{Parents:first, sinned against God ``f10!} being left to the freedom of\index{Causation:will
of creatures:free ``f10!} their own will, through the temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of Satan,

``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 3:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.   6-8,

``f10!} as a public person, not for himself only, but for his posterity\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from

Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 24 \textit{What is sin?}

A. Sin is\index{Sin:defined ``f10!} any want of conformity unto, or transgression of\index{God's
law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}, any law of God, given as a rule\index{God's law:moral:rule for obedience
``f10!} to the reasonable\index{Mankind:created:reasonable soul ``f10!} creature\index{creatures ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1
John 3:4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0,
12\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 25 \textit{Wherein consists the sinfulness of that estate whereinto}\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and misery
``f10!}\textit{ man fell}\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sinfulness of that estate whereinto\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and misery ``f10!} man

Adam) ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg.
``f30!}, 19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, 19, pg. ``f30!}.} the want of that righteousness
wherein\index{Sin:original:original righteousness corrupted ``f10!} he was created\index{Mankind:created:state ``f10!},
and the corruption of his\index{Sin:original:corrupt nature:whole ``f10!} nature, whereby he is utterly
indisposed\index{Sin:original:utterly indisposed ``f10!}, disabled\index{Sin:original:utterly unable and unwilling to
do will of God ``f10!}, and made opposite unto all that is spiritually good, and\index{Sin:original:lost all spiritual
good ``f10!} wholly inclined\index{Sin:original:inclined to do evil ``f10!} to all evil, and that
continually;\footnote{\ Romans 3:10\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v. 
10-19, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  
7, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1-3, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 6:5\index{01 Genesis:ch.   6, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}.} which is commonly called Original\index{Sin:original:source of all transgressions ``f10!} Sin, and from which
do proceed all\index{Sin:original:proceeds all transgressions ``f10!} actual transgressions\index{God's
law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}.\footnote{\ James 1:14\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}{}-15\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 26 \textit{How is original sin conveyed from our first parents}\index{Parents:first, sinned against God
``f10!}\textit{ unto their posterity}\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending from Adam ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Original\index{Sin:original:source of all transgressions ``f10!} sin is conveyed from our first
parents\index{Parents:first, sinned against God ``f10!} unto their posterity\index{Sin:original:all mankind descending
from Adam ``f10!} by natural generation, so\index{Sin:original:by ordinary generation ``f10!} as all that proceed from
the\index{Holy Spirit:procession from Father and Son ``f10!}m in that way are conceived
and\index{Sin:original:conceived and born in ``f10!} born in sin.\footnote{\ Psalm 51:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.  
5, pg. ``f30!}; Job 14:4\index{18 Job:ch.  14, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Job 15:14\index{18 Job:ch.  15, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}; John 3:6\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 27 \textit{What misery}\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}\textit{ did the fall}\index{Sin:original:first transgression

A. The fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!} brought upon mankind\index{Sin:original:all mankind

liable\index{Punishment:just:result of Adam's sin ``f10!} to all punishments\index{Punishment:temporal:evils that

v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}, 46\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41,
