Q. 28 \textit{What are the punishment}\index{Punishment:of sin ``f10!}\textit{s}\index{Punishment:temporal:evils that
befall us ``f10!}\textit{ of sin in this world?}

A. The punishments\index{Punishment:temporal:evils that befall us ``f10!} of sin in this world are either inward,
as\index{Punishment:temporal:inward instance classes ``f10!} blindness\index{blindness, spiritual ``f10!} of
mind,\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} a
reprobate\index{Punishment:temporal:reprobate sense ``f10!} sense,\footnote{\ Romans 1:28\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v. 
28, pg. ``f30!}.} strong delusions\index{Punishment:temporal:delusions ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians
2:11\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} hardness of heart\index{Heart:hardened
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 2:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} horror of
conscience\index{Conscience:horror of ``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah 33:14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  33, v.  14, pg. ``f30!};
Genesis 4:13\index{01 Genesis:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 27:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}.} and vile affections\index{Sexual immorality:vile ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 1:26\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v. 
26, pg. ``f30!}.} or outward, as\index{Punishment:temporal:outward instance classes ``f10!} the curse of
God\index{Curse:of God ``f10!} upon the creatures\index{creatures ``f10!} for our sakes,\footnote{\ Genesis
3:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} and all other evils that befall us in our bodies, names, estates,
relations, and employments\index{Punishment:temporal:aspects of life ``f10!};\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 28:15-18\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.  28, v.  15-18, pg. ``f30!}.} together with death\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!}
itself.\footnote{\ Romans 6:21, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  21, 23, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 29 \textit{What are the punishment}\index{Punishment:of sin ``f10!}\textit{s}\index{Punishment:temporal:evils that
befall us ``f10!}\textit{ of sin in the world to come?}

A. The punishments\index{Punishment:temporal:evils that befall us ``f10!} of sin in the world to come, are everlasting
separation\index{Punishment:everlasting:separation from God ``f10!} from the comfortable presence of God, and most
grievous torments in\index{Punishment:everlasting:torments (body and soul) ``f10!} soul and body, without
intermission\index{Punishment:hell:no intermission ``f10!}, in hell\index{Hell:hell ``f10!} fire\index{Hell:fire
``f10!} forever.\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 1:9\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 9:43-44,
46, 48\index{41 Mark:ch.   9, v.  43-44, 46, 48, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 16:24\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 30 \textit{Does God leave all mankind}\index{Mankind:not all left to perish in sin and misery ``f10!}\textit{ to
perish}\index{Redemption:not all perish ``f10!}\textit{ in the estate of sin}\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and
misery ``f10!}\textit{ and misery}\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. God does not leave all men to perish\index{Redemption:not all perish ``f10!} in the estate of
sin\index{Sin:original:an estate of sin and misery ``f10!} and misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1
Thessalonians 5:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} into which they fell\index{Sin:original:all
mankind descending from Adam ``f10!} by the breach of the\index{God's law:breach:first covenant ``f10!} first covenant,
commonly called the Covenant of Works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!};\footnote{\ Galatians 3:10\index{48
Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} but of his mere love
and\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!} mercy delivers\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!} his
elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} out of it, and brings them into an estate of salvation\index{Salvation:belief
in Jesus by faith ``f10!} by the second covenant\index{Covenant:second ``f10!}, commonly called the Covenant of
Grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Titus 3:4-7\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   4-7, pg. ``f30!};
Galatians 3:21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}{}-22\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20-22, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 31 \textit{With whom was the covenant of grace}\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}\textit{ made?}

A. The covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!} was made with Christ as the second Adam\index{Jesus:second
Adam ``f10!}, and in him with all the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} as his seed\index{Election:God's seed
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5-21\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  15-21, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 53:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.  10,
pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 32 \textit{How is the grace}\index{Covenant:grace:manifested ``f10!}\textit{ of God
manifested}\index{Grace:manifested ``f10!}\textit{ in the second covenant}\index{Covenant:second ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The grace of God\index{Covenant:grace:manifested ``f10!} is manifested\index{Grace:manifested ``f10!} in the second
covenant\index{Covenant:second ``f10!}, in that he freely\index{Salvation:freely offered ``f10!} provides and offers to
sinners a Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!},\footnote{\ Genesis 3:15\index{01 Genesis:ch.   3, v.  15,
pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 42:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  42, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:27\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  27, pg.
``f30!}.} and life and salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} by him;\footnote{\ 1 John
5:11-12\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.} and requiring\index{Salvation:faith alone required ``f10!}
faith as the condition\index{Faith:necessary for salvation ``f10!} to interest them\index{Faith:required for interest
(share) in Christ ``f10!}\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{43 John:ch.   1, v. 
12, pg. ``f30!}; John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} in him, promises\index{Covenant:promises
``f10!} and gives his Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}\footnote{\ Proverbs 1:23\index{20 Proverbs:ch. 
1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} to all his elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}, to work in them that
faith\index{Faith:worked in believers by the Holy Spirit ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 4:13\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} with all other saving graces\index{Grace:of salvation
``f10!};\footnote{\ Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2-23\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v. 
22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} and to enable\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} them unto all
holy\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} obedience,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  27,
pg. ``f30!}.} as the evidence of the truth of their faith\index{Faith:evidenced by obedience ``f10!}\footnote{\ James
2:18, 22\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  18, 22, pg. ``f30!}.} and thankfulness\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!} to
God,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:14-15\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}.} and as the way which he
has appointed them to salvation.\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 33 \textit{Was the covenant of grace}\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}\textit{ always administered after one and
the same manner?}

A. The covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!} was not always administered after the same manner, but the
administrations of it\index{Covenant:administrations ``f10!} under the Old Testament\index{Scripture:Old Testament
``f10!} were different from those under the New.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 3:6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6,
pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6-9, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 34 \textit{How was the covenant of grace}\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}\textit{ administered under the Old
Testament}\index{Scripture:Old Testament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!} was administered under the Old Testament\index{Scripture:Old
Testament ``f10!}, by promises\index{Covenant:promises ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 15:8\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   8,
pg. ``f30!}.} prophecies\index{Covenant:prophecies ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 3:20, 24\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  20, 24,
pg. ``f30!}.} sacrifices\index{Ceremonial law:sacrifices ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v. 
1, pg. ``f30!}.} circumcision\index{circumcision ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 4:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}.} the passover\index{passover ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 5:7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   7, pg.
``f30!}.} and other types\index{types, OT ``f10!} and ordinances, which\index{Covenant:OT ordinances:signified Christ
``f10!} did all fore signify Christ then to come, and were for that time sufficient to\index{Covenant:OT
ordinances:sufficient for that time ``f10!} build up the\index{Holy Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!}
elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} in faith\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ, as Messiah ``f10!} in the
promised\index{Jesus:Messiah promised ``f10!} Messiah,\footnote{\ Hebrews 8-10\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 8-10, pg. ``f30!};
Hebrews 11:13\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} by whom they then had full
remission\index{Redemption:remission of sins ``f10!} of sin, and eternal salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by
faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:7-9, 14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.   7-9, 14, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 35 \textit{How is the covenant of grace}\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}\textit{ administered under the New
Testament}\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Under the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}, when Christ the substance was exhibited,
the\index{Covenant:grace:exhibited ``f10!} same covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!} was and still is
to be administered\index{Covenant:grace:administered through preaching of word ``f10!} in the preaching of the
word,\footnote{\ Mark 16:15\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and the
administration\index{Church:true:sacraments administered ``f10!} of the sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances
``f10!} of Baptism\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch. 
28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}.} and the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg.
``f30!}{}-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23-25, pg. ``f30!}.} in which grace\index{Grace:exhibited in
sacraments ``f10!} and salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} are held forth in more
fulness\index{Covenant:new:more fulness ``f10!}, evidence, and efficacy, to\index{Sacraments:spiritual efficacy ``f10!}
all nations\index{Gospel:to all nations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 3:6\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6,
pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   6-9, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 8:6, 10-11\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   8, v. 
6, 10-11, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 36 \textit{Who is the Mediator}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{ of the covenant of
grace}\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The only Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} of the covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace
``f10!} is the Lord Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 2:5\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} who, being
the eternal\index{Jesus:eternal Son ``f10!} Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God, of one substance\index{God's
attributes:trinity:one substance ``f10!} and equal with the\index{God's attributes:trinity:persons equal ``f10!}
Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 14\index{43
John:ch.   1, v.   1, 14, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:30\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 2:6\index{50
Philippians:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} in the fulness of time\index{Jesus:incarnation:in fulness of time ``f10!}
became man,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} and so was and
continues\index{Jesus:God-man ``f10!} to be God and man, in two entire distinct natures\index{Jesus:two distinct
natures ``f10!}, and one person, forever.\footnote{\ Luke 1:35\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  35, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
9:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:9\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!};
Hebrews 7:24-25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 37 \textit{How did Christ, being the Son}\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}\textit{ of God, become man?}

A. Christ the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God became man, by taking to himself a true body, and a
reasonable\index{Jesus:human nature:reasonable soul ``f10!} soul,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:38\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}.}
being conceived by\index{Jesus:conceived:by the power of the Holy Spirit ``f10!} the power of the Holy Ghost\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!} in the womb\index{Jesus:conceived:in womb of virgin Mary ``f10!} of the
virgin\index{Jesus:born of virgin Mary ``f10!} Mary\index{Mary, mother of Jesus ``f10!}, of her
substance\index{Jesus:conceived:of Mary's substance ``f10!}, and born of her,\footnote{\ Luke 1:27, 31, 35\index{42
Luke:ch.   1, v.  27, 31, 35, pg. ``f30!}, 42\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  27, 31, 35, 42, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} yet without sin.\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  
4, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 7:26\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 38 \textit{Why was it requisite that}\index{Jesus:mediator:requisite that he be both God and man ``f10!}\textit{ the
Mediator}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{ should be God?}

A. It was requisite that\index{Jesus:mediator:requisite that he be both God and man ``f10!} the
Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} should be God, that he might sustain and keep the human nature
from\index{Jesus:human nature:sustained by God ``f10!} sinking under the infinite\index{God's attributes:infinite:wrath
``f10!} wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}, and the power of death\index{Jesus:death:under power of
``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts. 2:24-25; Romans 1:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:25\index{45
Romans:ch.   4, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 9:14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} give worth
and\index{Jesus:worth of his sufferings ``f10!} efficacy to his\index{Redemption:efficacy of Christ's incarnation
``f10!} sufferings, obedience\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}, and intercession\index{Jesus:in
heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts 20:28\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  28, pg. ``f30!};
Hebrews 7:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25-28, pg. ``f30!};
Hebrews 9:14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and to satisfy God's justice\index{Jesus:satisfied divine
justice ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24,
pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24-26, pg. ``f30!}.} procure his favor\index{Jesus:favour with the Father
``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 3:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  
3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} purchase\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!} a peculiar people,\footnote{\ Titus.
2:13-14.} give his Spirit to them,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:6\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}
conquer\index{Jesus:conqueror of his and our enemies ``f10!} all their enemies\index{Enemies:of believers overcome
``f10!},\footnote{\ Luke 1:6\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}8-69, 71, 74\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  68-69,
71, 74, pg. ``f30!}.} and bring them to everlasting\index{Salvation:everlasting ``f10!}
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 5:8-9\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.  
8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 9:11-15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  11-15, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 39 \textit{Why was it requisite that}\index{Jesus:mediator:requisite that he be both God and man ``f10!}\textit{ the
Mediator}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{ should be man?}

A. It was requisite that\index{Jesus:mediator:requisite that he be both God and man ``f10!} the
Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} should be man, that he might advance\index{Jesus:mediator:advances
human nature ``f10!} our nature,\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} perform obedience\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!} to the
law,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} suffer and\index{Jesus:death:sufferings
and death ``f10!} make intercession\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!} for us in our
nature,\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 7:24-25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} have a fellow feeling\index{Jesus:fellow
feelings with our infirmities ``f10!} of our infirmities;\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:infirmities
``f10!}\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} that we might receive the
adoption\index{Adoption:in salvation ``f10!} of sons,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:5\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}.} and have comfort\index{Faith:source of comfort ``f10!} and access with\index{Believers:bold access to God's
throne ``f10!} boldness\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!} unto the throne of grace\index{Grace:throne of
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:16\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 40 \textit{Why was it requisite that}\index{Jesus:mediator:requisite that he be both God and man ``f10!}\textit{ the
Mediator}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{ should be God and man in one person?}

A. It was requisite that\index{Jesus:mediator:requisite that he be both God and man ``f10!} the
Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}, who was to reconcile\index{Jesus:purchased reconciliation ``f10!}
God and man, should himself be both God and man, and this in one person, that the proper works\index{Jesus:proper works
of each nature ``f10!} of each nature might be accepted of\index{Jesus:accepted of God ``f10!} God for us, and
relied\index{Jesus:mediator:relied on by us for salvation ``f10!} on by us,\footnote{\ Matthew 1:21\index{40
Matthew:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{40 Matthew:ch.   1, v.  21, 23, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 3:17\index{40
Matthew:ch.   3, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 9:14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} as the works of the
whole person.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:6\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 41 \textit{Why was our Mediator}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{ called
Jesus}\index{Jesus:mediator:named Jesus ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Our Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} was called Jesus\index{Jesus:mediator:named Jesus ``f10!},
because he saves\index{Jesus:saviour of the Church ``f10!} his people from their sins.\footnote{\ Matthew 1:21\index{40
Matthew:ch.   1, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 42 \textit{Why was our Mediator}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{ called Christ?}

A. Our Mediator\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!} was called Christ, because he was anointed\index{Jesus:anointed
with Holy Spirit ``f10!} with the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!} above measure;\footnote{\ John
3:3\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 45:7\index{19
Psalms:ch.  45, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} and so set apart, and fully furnished\index{Jesus:mediator:fully furnished to
execute office ``f10!} with all authority and ability,\footnote{\ John 6:27\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  27, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 28:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}.} to
execute the office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!}s of prophet\index{Jesus:prophet:office ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts
3:21\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}{}-22\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 4:18,
21\index{42 Luke:ch.   4, v.  18, 21, pg. ``f30!}.} priest,\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:14-15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v. 
14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:5-7\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.   5-7, pg. ``f30!}.} and king\index{Jesus:King ``f10!}
of his church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 2:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
21:5\index{40 Matthew:ch.  21, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 9:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.   6, pg.
``f30!}{}-7\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   9, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 2:8\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg.
``f30!}{}-11\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   8-11, pg. ``f30!}.} in the estate both of his humiliation
and\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!} exaltation\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!}.


\bigskip

Q. 43 \textit{How does Christ execute the office}\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!}\textit{ of a
prophet}\index{Jesus:prophet:office ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ executes the office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} of a prophet\index{Jesus:prophet:office ``f10!}, in his
revealing\index{Revelation:God's word ``f10!} to the church,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}8\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} in all ages, by\index{Church:universal ``f10!} his Spirit and
word,\footnote{\ 1 Peter 1:10-12\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} in divers ways of
administration\index{Jesus:prophet:administration ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} the whole will of God,\footnote{\ John 15:15\index{43
John:ch.  15, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} in all things concerning their edification and\index{Holy Spirit:edification of
believers ``f10!} salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 20:32\index{44 Acts:ch. 
20, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{49 Ephesians:ch.  
4, v.  11-13, pg. ``f30!}; John 20:31\index{43 John:ch.  20, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 44 \textit{How does Christ execute the office}\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!}\textit{ of a priest?}

A. Christ executes the office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} of a priest, in his\index{Jesus:priest ``f10!} once offering
himself\index{Jesus:sacrifice:of himself ``f10!} a sacrifice without spot\index{Jesus:sacrifice:without spot ``f10!} to
God,\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 28\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  14, 28,
pg. ``f30!}.} to be a reconciliation\index{Jesus:purchased reconciliation ``f10!} for the sins of his
people;\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.} and in making continual intercession\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!} for
them.\footnote{\ Hebrews 7:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 45 \textit{How does Christ execute the office}\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!}\textit{ of a king}\index{Jesus:King
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ executes the office\index{Jesus:offices ``f10!} of a king\index{Jesus:King ``f10!}, in calling
out\index{Effectual call:elect ``f10!} of the world a people to himself,\footnote{\ Acts 15:14-16\index{44 Acts:ch. 
15, v.  14-16, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 4:4-5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   4, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 49:10\index{01
Genesis:ch.  49, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 110:3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 110, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and giving them
officers\index{Church officers:officers ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}{}-12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:28\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.
28, pg. ``f30!}.} laws,\footnote{\ Isaiah 33:22\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  33, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} and censures,
by\index{Church discipline:censures ``f10!} which he visibly governs\index{Providence:governing all ``f10!}
them;\footnote{\ Matthew 18:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  17-18,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 5:4-5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} in bestowing saving
grace\index{Grace:of salvation ``f10!} upon his elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 5:3\index{44
Acts:ch.   5, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}1\index{44 Acts:ch.   5, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} rewarding their
obedience,\index{Believers:obedience:rewarded ``f10!}\footnote{\ Revelation 2:1\index{66 Revelation:ch.   2, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}0\index{66 Revelation:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 22:12\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  12,
pg. ``f30!}.} and correcting them for\index{Jesus:corrects believers ``f10!} their sins,\footnote{\ Revelation
3:1\index{66 Revelation:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9\index{66 Revelation:ch.   3, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} preserving and
supporting\index{Temptation:believers supported by Christ during ``f10!} them under all their
temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} and sufferings,\footnote{\ Isaiah 63:9\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  63, v.   9,
pg. ``f30!}.} restraining\index{Enemies:of believers restrained ``f10!} and overcoming\index{Jesus:conqueror of his and
our enemies ``f10!} all their enemies\index{Enemies:of believers overcome ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians
15:25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 110:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 110, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 110, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} and powerfully ordering all\index{Providence:ordering:all
things for his glory and believers' good ``f10!} things for his own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 14:10-11\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} and their good;\footnote{\ Romans
8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} and also in taking
vengeance\index{Jesus:judge:taking vengeance ``f10!} on the rest, who know not God, and obey not\index{Punishment:those
who do not obey the Gospel ``f10!} the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 1:8-9\index{53 2
Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 2:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{19
Psalms:ch.   2, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 46 \textit{What was the estate of Christ's humiliation}\index{Jesus:humiliation:estate ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The estate of Christ's humiliation\index{Jesus:humiliation:estate ``f10!} was that low
condition\index{Jesus:humiliation:low condition ``f10!}, wherein he for our sakes,
emptying\index{Jesus:humiliation:emptying himself of glory ``f10!} himself of his glory, took\index{Jesus:glory ``f10!}
upon him the form of a servant\index{Jesus:humiliation:took on form of a servant ``f10!}, in his
conception\index{Jesus:humiliation:conception ``f10!} and birth\index{Jesus:birth ``f10!}, life, death, and
after\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} his death, until his resurrection\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Philippians 2:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2,
v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:31\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 8:9\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   8, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:24\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 47 \textit{How did Christ humble himself}\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!}\textit{ in his
conception}\index{Jesus:humiliation:conception ``f10!}\textit{ and birth}\index{Jesus:birth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ humbled himself\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!} in his
conception\index{Jesus:humiliation:conception ``f10!} and birth\index{Jesus:birth ``f10!}, in that, being from all
eternity\index{God's attributes:eternal ``f10!} the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God, in the bosom of the
Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, he was pleased\index{Providence:at God's pleasure ``f10!} in the fulness of
time\index{Jesus:incarnation:in fulness of time ``f10!} to become the son of man, made of a woman of low
estate\index{Jesus:born of woman of low estate ``f10!}, and to be born of\index{Jesus:born of virgin Mary ``f10!} her;
with divers circumstances of more than ordinary abasement\index{Jesus:humiliation:abasement ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John
1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 18\index{43 John:ch.   1,
v.  14, 18, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 2:7\index{42 Luke:ch.   2,
v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 48 \textit{How did Christ humble himself}\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!}\textit{ in his life?}

A. Christ humbled himself\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!} in his life, by
subjecting\index{Jesus:humiliation:subjected himself to the law ``f10!} himself to the law,\footnote{\ Galatians
4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} which he perfectly fulfil\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law
``f10!}led;\footnote{\ Matthew 5:17\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}9\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} and by conflicting\index{Jesus:conflicted
with:indignities of world ``f10!} with the indignities\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:indignities ``f10!} of the
world,\footnote{\ Psalm 22:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  22, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!} of
Satan,\footnote{\ Matthew 4:1-12\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   1-12, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 4:13\index{42 Luke:ch.   4, v. 
13, pg. ``f30!}.} and infirmities in\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:infirmities ``f10!} his flesh, whether common to
the nature of man, or particularly accompanying that his low condition\index{Jesus:humiliation:low condition
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}{}-18\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 4:15\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  15, pg.
``f30!}; Isaiah 52:13-14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  52, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 49 \textit{How did Christ humble himself}\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!}\textit{ in his
death}\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ humbled himself\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!} in his death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}, in
that having been betrayed\index{Jesus:betrayed ``f10!} by Judas\index{Judas ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 27:4\index{40
Matthew:ch.  27, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} forsaken by\index{Jesus:forsaken by disciples ``f10!} his
disciples\index{disciples of Jesus ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 26:56\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  56, pg. ``f30!}.}
scorned\index{Jesus:humiliation:scorned ``f10!} and rejected\index{Jesus:humiliation:rejected by world ``f10!} by the
world,\footnote{\ Isaiah 53:2-3\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} condemned by\index{Jesus:condemned by
wicked men ``f10!} Pilate\index{Pilate ``f10!}, and tormented\index{Jesus:humiliation:tormented ``f10!} by his
persecutors\index{Jesus:humiliation:persecuted ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 27:26-50\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v. 
26-50, pg. ``f30!}; John 19:34\index{43 John:ch.  19, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}.} having also
conflicted\index{Jesus:conflicted with:terror of death ``f10!} with the terrors of death\index{Jesus:death:terrors of
``f10!}, and the powers of darkness\index{darkness, spiritual ``f10!}, felt and borne the weight of God's
wrath,\index{Wrath:of God:borne by Jesus as sin offering ``f10!}\footnote{\ Luke 22:44\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  44,
pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 27:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v.  46, pg.
``f30!}.} he laid down\index{Jesus:laid down life as sin offering ``f10!} his life an offering
for\index{Jesus:sacrifice:offering for sin ``f10!} sin,\footnote{\ Isaiah 53:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}.} enduring the painful\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered pain ``f10!},
shameful\index{Jesus:humiliation:suffered:shameful death of cross ``f10!}, and cursed\index{Jesus:death:cursed ``f10!}
death of the cross\index{Jesus:death:on cross ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Philippians 2:8\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   8,
pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:13\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v. 
13, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 50 \textit{Wherein consisted}\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!}\textit{ Christ's humiliation after his
death}\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ's humiliation after\index{Jesus:humiliation:aspects of ``f10!} his death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!}
consisted in his being buried\index{Jesus:buried ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:3-4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
15, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.} and continuing\index{Jesus:death:continuing under power for time ``f10!} in the state of
the dead, and under the power of death\index{Jesus:death:under power of ``f10!} till the third
day\index{Jesus:resurrection:third day ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm 16:10\index{19 Psalms:ch.  16, v.  10, pg. ``f30!};
Acts 2:24\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-27, 31\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  24-27, 31, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
6:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 12:40\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  40, pg. ``f30!}.} which
has been otherwise expressed in these words, he descended\index{Jesus:descended into hell ``f10!} into
hell\index{Hell:hell ``f10!}. 


\bigskip

Q. 51 \textit{What was the estate of Christ's exaltation}\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The estate of Christ's exaltation\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!} comprehends his
resurrection\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
15, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} ascension\index{Jesus:ascension:into heaven ``f10!},\footnote{\ Mark 16:19\index{41 Mark:ch. 
16, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} sitting\index{Jesus:in heaven:sitting at right hand of Father ``f10!} at the right hand of
the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}
and his coming again to judge the\index{Jesus:judge:world ``f10!} world.\footnote{\ Acts 1:11\index{44 Acts:ch.   1, v.
11, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 17:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 52 \textit{How was Christ exalted}\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!}\textit{ in his
resurrection}\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ was exalted\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!} in his resurrection\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!},
in that, not having seen corruption\index{Jesus:death:no corruption ``f10!} in death (of which it was not possible for
him to be held),\footnote{\ Acts 2:24\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}, 27\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  24, 27,
pg. ``f30!}.} and having the very same body in which he suffered\index{Jesus:resurrection:body same:in which he
suffered ``f10!}, with the essential properties thereof\index{Jesus:resurrection:body same:essential properties
``f10!}\footnote{\ Luke 24:39\index{42 Luke:ch.  24, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} (but without
mortality\index{Jesus:resurrection:body:immortal ``f10!}, and other common infirmities
belonging\index{Jesus:resurrection:freed from infirmities ``f10!} to this life), really united to
his\index{Jesus:resurrection:body same:united to his soul ``f10!} soul,\footnote{\ Romans 6:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   6,
v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 1:18\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} he
rose\index{Jesus:resurrection:third day ``f10!} again from the dead the third day by his own
power\index{Jesus:resurrection:by his own power ``f10!};\footnote{\ John 10:18\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}.} whereby he declared\index{Jesus:resurrection:declared Son of God ``f10!} himself to be the
Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!} of God,\footnote{\ Romans 1:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.} to have
satisfied divine justice\index{God's attributes:administers justice ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch. 
8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  34, pg. ``f30!}.} to have vanquished\index{Jesus:death:vanquished
``f10!} death, and him that had the power\index{Satan:vanquished by Christ ``f10!} of it,\footnote{\ Hebrews
2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and to be Lord of
quick and dead\index{Jesus:lord of quick and dead ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Romans 14:9\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v.   9, pg.
``f30!}.} all which he did as a public person,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:21-22\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v. 
21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} the head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!} of his church\index{Church:Christ's
``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}, 22-23\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1,
v.  20, 22-23, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} for their
justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 4:25\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  25, pg.
``f30!}.} quickening in grace,\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:1\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, 5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.
2, v.   1, 5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:12\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} support against
enemies\index{Enemies:believers delivered from ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15,
v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  25-27, pg. ``f30!}.} and to
assure\index{Jesus:resurrection:assures of believers' resurrection ``f10!} them of their
resurrection\index{Resurrection:believers:assurance of ``f10!} from the dead at the last day\index{Last day:last day
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:20\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 53 \textit{How was Christ exalted}\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!}\textit{ in his
ascension}\index{Jesus:ascension:into heaven ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ was exalted\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!} in his ascension\index{Jesus:ascension:into heaven ``f10!}, in that
having after his resurrection\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!} often
appeared\index{Jesus:post-resurrection appearances ``f10!} unto and conversed\index{Believers:conversed with apostles
``f10!} with his apostles\index{Apostles:apostles ``f10!}, speaking to them of the things pertaining to the kingdom of
God\index{Kingdom of God:Kingdom of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 1:2-3\index{44 Acts:ch.   1, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.}
and giving them commission\index{Apostles:commissioned to preach the Gospel ``f10!} to preach
the\index{Preaching:Gospel ``f10!} gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!} to all nations\index{Gospel:to all nations
``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v. 
19-20, pg. ``f30!}.} forty\index{Jesus:ascension:forty days after resurrection ``f10!} days after his resurrection, he,
in our nature, and as our head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:20\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6,
v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} triumphing\index{Jesus:ascension:triumph over enemies ``f10!} over
enemies\index{Enemies:triumphed over by Christ ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   8,
pg. ``f30!}.} visibly went\index{Jesus:resurrection:visible ``f10!} up into the highest heavens, there to receive gifts
for\index{Jesus:ascension:receive gifts for men ``f10!} men,\footnote{\ Acts 1:9-11\index{44 Acts:ch.   1, v.   9-11,
pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:10\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 68:18\index{19 Psalms:ch.  68, v. 
18, pg. ``f30!}.} to raise up our affections thither\index{Worship:affections directed to God
``f10!},\footnote{\ Colossians 3:1-2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} and to prepare
a\index{Jesus:preparing a place in heaven for believers ``f10!} place for us,\footnote{\ John 14:3\index{43 John:ch. 
14, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} where himself is, and shall continue till his second coming\index{Jesus:second coming ``f10!}
at the end of the world.\footnote{\ Acts 3:21\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 54 \textit{How is Christ exalted}\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!}\textit{ in his sitting}\index{Jesus:in
heaven:sitting at right hand of Father ``f10!}\textit{ at the right hand of God?}

A. Christ is exalted\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!} in his sitting\index{Jesus:in heaven:sitting at right hand of Father
``f10!} at the right hand of God, in that as God-man\index{Jesus:God-man ``f10!} he is advanced to the highest favor
with\index{Jesus:favour with the Father ``f10!} God the Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!},\footnote{\ Philippians
2:9\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} with all fulness of joy\index{Joy:everlasting
``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 2:28\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 16:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  16, v.  11,
pg. ``f30!}.} glory,\footnote{\ John 17:5\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and power over\index{God's
attributes:almighty power ``f10!} all things in heaven\index{Jesus:ruler over heaven and earth ``f10!} and
earth;\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:22\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:22\index{60 1 Peter:ch.  
3, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} and does gather and defend\index{Jesus:defends his Church ``f10!} his
church\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}, and subdue the\index{Prayer:for God to subdue the flesh (sin in the world)
``f10!}ir enemies; furnishes his ministers\index{Church officers:minsters ``f10!} and people with
gifts\index{Church:furnished with:gifts and graces ``f10!} and graces,\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:10\index{49 Ephesians:ch.
4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 110:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 110,
v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} and makes intercession\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!} for
them.\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  34, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 55 \textit{How does Christ make intercession}\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ makes intercession\index{Jesus:in heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!}, by his appearing
in\index{Jesus:incarnation:appearing in our nature ``f10!} our nature continually before the Father\index{Father:God
the ``f10!} in heaven,\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}, 24\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  
9, v.  12, 24, pg. ``f30!}.} in the merit of\index{Jesus:obedience:merit of ``f10!} his obedience and sacrifice
on\index{Jesus:sacrifice:of himself ``f10!} earth,\footnote{\ Hebrews 1:3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}.} declaring\index{Revelation:special declaration ``f10!} his will to have it applied to all
believers;\footnote{\ John 3:16\index{43 John:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; John 17:9\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   9,
pg. ``f30!}, 20\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   9, 20, pg. ``f30!}, 24\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.   9, 20, 24, pg. ``f30!}.}
answering all accusations against them,\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45
Romans:ch.   8, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  33-34, pg. ``f30!}.} and procuring for them quiet
of conscience\index{Conscience:quiet ``f10!}, notwithstanding daily failings\index{God's law:broken daily by all men
(thought, word, deed) ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{45
Romans:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 2:1-2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} access
with\index{Believers:bold access to God's throne ``f10!} boldness\index{Prayer:with boldness ``f10!} to the throne of
grace\index{Grace:throne of ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 4:16\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} and
acceptance of\index{Believers:accepted in Christ ``f10!} their persons\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch. 
1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and services.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 2:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 56 \textit{How is Christ to be exalted}\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!}\textit{ in his coming again to judge
the}\index{Jesus:judge:world ``f10!}\textit{ world?}

A. Christ is to be exalted\index{Jesus:exaltation ``f10!} in his coming again to judge the\index{Jesus:judge:world
``f10!} world, in that he, who was unjustly judged and\index{Jesus:judged and condemned unjustly ``f10!} condemned
by\index{Jesus:condemned by wicked men ``f10!} wicked men,\footnote{\ Acts 3:14-15\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  14-15,
pg. ``f30!}.} shall come again at the last day\index{Last day:last day ``f10!} in great power\index{Jesus:return:in
great power ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 24:30\index{40 Matthew:ch.  24, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} and in the full
manifestation of his own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}, and of his Father\index{Father:God the
``f10!}{}'s, with all his holy\index{Angels:holy ``f10!} angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!},\footnote{\ Luke
9:26\index{42 Luke:ch.   9, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:31\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} with a
shout\index{Jesus:return:with shout and voice of archangel ``f10!}, with the voice of the\index{Angels:voice of, at
judgement day ``f10!} archangel\index{Angels:archangel ``f10!}, and with the trumpet\index{Last day:trumpet ``f10!} of
God,\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 4:16\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} to judge the world in
righteousness\index{Judgement day:in righteousness ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts 17:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  31, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 57 \textit{What benefits has}\index{Believers:benefits:of Christ's mediation ``f10!}\textit{ Christ procured by his
mediation}\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Christ, by his mediation\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}, has procured\index{Believers:benefits:of
redemption ``f10!} redemption,\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} with all other
benefits of the\index{Covenant:grace:benefits ``f10!} covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 1:20\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 58 \textit{How do we come to be made partakers of the benefits which Christ}\index{Believers:benefits:Christ procured
``f10!}\textit{ has procured}\index{Believers:benefits:of redemption ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. We are made partakers\index{Redemption:partakers through Christ ``f10!} of the benefits which
Christ\index{Believers:benefits:Christ procured ``f10!} has procured\index{Believers:benefits:of redemption
``f10!},\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1-12\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  11-12, pg.
``f30!}.} by the application of them unto us, which is the work especially of God the Holy Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy
Ghost ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Titus 3:5\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5-6,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 59 \textit{Who are made partakers}\index{Redemption:partakers through Christ ``f10!}\textit{ of redemption through
Christ?}

A. Redemption is certainly applied, and effectually communicated\index{Redemption:effectually:communicated ``f10!}, to
all those for whom Christ has purchased\index{Redemption:purchased by Christ ``f10!} it;\footnote{\ Ephesians
1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:37\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}, 39\index{43 John:ch.  
6, v.  37, 39, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:15-16\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} who are in time by the Holy
Ghost\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!} enabled to believe\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:enables belief ``f10!} in
Christ according to the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  
8, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 4:13\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 60 \textit{Can they who have never heard the}\index{Salvation:none where Gospel not heard ``f10!}\textit{
gospel}\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}\textit{, and so know not Jesus Christ, nor believe in him, be saved by
their}\index{Salvation:not by:living according to light of nature ``f10!}\textit{ living according to the light of
nature?}

A. They who, having never heard the\index{Salvation:none where Gospel not heard ``f10!} gospel\index{Gospel:gospel
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}.} know not Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ 2 Thessalonians 1:8-9\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg.
``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg.
``f30!}; John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0-12\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  10-12, pg. ``f30!}.} and
believe not in him, cannot be saved,\footnote{\ John 8:24\index{43 John:ch.   8, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}; Mark
16:16\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} be they never so diligent to\index{God's law:diligence in
application ``f10!} frame their\index{Salvation:not by:obedience ``f10!} lives according to the light of
nature,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0-24\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.
1, v.  20-24, pg. ``f30!}.} or the laws of that religion which they profess\index{Profession:of false religion
``f10!};\footnote{\ John 4:22\index{43 John:ch.   4, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:31-32\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v. 
31-32, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:4-9\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.   4-9, pg. ``f30!}.} neither is there
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} in any other, but in Christ alone,\footnote{\ Acts
4:12\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} who is the Savior\index{Jesus:saviour of the Church ``f10!} only of
his body the church\index{Church:Christ's body ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2,
pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 61 \textit{Are all they saved who}\index{Salvation:not for all who hear the gospel ``f10!}\textit{ hear the
gospel}\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}\textit{, and live in the church}\index{Church:home of believers ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. All that hear the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}, and live in the visible church\index{Church:visible ``f10!},
are not saved; but\index{Salvation:not for all who hear the gospel ``f10!} they only who are true members of
the\index{Church members ``f10!} church invisible\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 12:38-40\index{43
John:ch.  12, v.  38-40, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:7\index{45
Romans:ch.  11, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 7:21\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 22:14\index{40
Matthew:ch.  22, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 62 \textit{What is the visible church}\index{Church:visible ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The visible church\index{Church:visible ``f10!} is a society made up of all such as in all ages and places of the
world do profess the true\index{Profession:of true religion ``f10!} religion,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 12:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  12, v.  13, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 15:9-12\index{45 Romans:ch.  15, v.   9-12, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 7:9\index{66 Revelation:ch.   7, v.   9, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 2:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 22:27-31\index{19 Psalms:ch.  22, v.  27-31, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 45:17\index{19 Psalms:ch.  45, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 59:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}1\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  59, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and of their children.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 7:14\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 11:16\index{45
Romans:ch.  11, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 63 \textit{What are the special privileges}\index{Believers:privileges ``f10!}\textit{ of the visible
church}\index{Church:visible ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The visible church\index{Church:visible ``f10!} has the privilege\index{Believers:privileges ``f10!} of being under
God's special care and government;\index{Church:Christ's ``f10!}\footnote{\ Isaiah 4:5-6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.   4, v.  
5-6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 4:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   4, v.  10,
pg. ``f30!}.} of being protected and\index{Church:protected in all ages by God ``f10!} preserved in
all\index{Church:preserved in all ages by God ``f10!} ages, not withstanding the opposition\index{Church:opposition
from enemies ``f10!} of all enemies\index{Enemies:of the Church ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm 115:1-2, 9\index{19
Psalms:ch. 115, v.   1-2, 9, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 31:4-5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  31, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Zechariah
12:2-4, 8-9\index{38 Zechariah:ch.  12, v.   2-4, 8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} and of enjoying the\index{Communion:enjoying
``f10!} communion of\index{Communion:of saints ``f10!} saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}, the ordinary means of
salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 2:39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  39, pg.
``f30!}, 42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  39, 42, pg. ``f30!}.} and offers of\index{Church:ordinary means of salvation
``f10!} grace by Christ\index{Church:furnished with:gifts and graces ``f10!} to all the members of\index{Church members
``f10!} it in the ministry\index{Gospel:ministry of ``f10!} of the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!},
testifying\index{Preachers:testify that all who believe will be saved ``f10!}, that whosoever believes in him shall be
saved,\footnote{\ Psalm 147:19-20\index{19 Psalms:ch. 147, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 9:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   9,
v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:11\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.
11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 16:15\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{41 Mark:ch.  16, v.  15-16, pg.
``f30!}.} and excluding\index{Salvation:no one excluded who comes to God ``f10!} none that will come unto
him.\footnote{\ John 6:37\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 64 \textit{What is the invisible church}\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} is the whole number of the elect\index{Election:elect of God
``f10!}, that have been, are, or shall be gathered\index{Church:universal ``f10!} into one under Christ the
head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!},
22-23\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  20, 22-23, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:16\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!};
John 11:52\index{43 John:ch.  11, v.  52, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 65 \textit{What special benefits do the}\index{Believers:benefits:as members of the Church ``f10!}\textit{ members of
the}\index{Church members ``f10!}\textit{ invisible church}\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}\textit{ enjoy by Christ?}

A. The members of the\index{Church members ``f10!} invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} by Christ enjoy union
and\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} communion with him\index{Communion:with Christ ``f10!} in grace
and glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:with Christ ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 17:2\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  
2, pg. ``f30!}1, 24\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  21, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5,
pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 66 \textit{What is that union which}\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!}\textit{ the
elect}\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}\textit{ have with Christ?}

A. The union which\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} have
with Christ is the work of God's grace\index{Grace:of salvation ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:22\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:6-8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby
they are spiritually\index{Believers:union with Christ:spiritually ``f10!} and mystically, yet really and
inseparably\index{Believers:union with Christ:inseparable ``f10!}, joined to Christ as their head\index{Church:Christ
as head ``f10!} and husband;\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 6:17\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; John
10:28\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}, 30\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  23, 30, pg. ``f30!}.}
which is done in their effectual calling\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 5:1\index{60 1
Peter:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   5, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 1:9\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 67 \textit{What is effectual calling}\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Effectual\index{Effectual call:calling ``f10!} calling is the work of God's almighty\index{God's attributes:almighty
power ``f10!} power and grace,\footnote{\ John 5:25\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:1\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8-20\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  18-20, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 1:8-9\index{55
2 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby (out\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} of his free and special love to
his\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!} elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}, and from nothing in them moving him
thereunto)\footnote{\ Titus. 3:4-5; Ephesians 2:4-5, 7-9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   4-5, 7-9, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
9:11\index{45 Romans:ch.   9, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} he does, in his accepted time\index{Salvation:at appointed time
``f10!}, invite\index{Effectual call:invitation to draw near to Christ ``f10!} and draw them\index{Effectual
call:drawing to Christ ``f10!} to Jesus Christ, by his word and Spirit\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit
``f10!};\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:20\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians
6:1-2\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:44\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  44, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Thessalonians 2:13\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v. 
13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} savingly enlightening\index{Effectual call:enlightening minds spiritually ``f10!} their
minds,\footnote{\ Acts 26:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 2:10, 12\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.} renewing and\index{Conversion:renewed by Holy Spirit ``f10!} powerfully
determining their\index{Effectual call:determining wills ``f10!} wills,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 11:19\index{26 Ezekiel:ch. 
11, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 36:26\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v. 
26-27, pg. ``f30!}; John 6:45\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  45, pg. ``f30!}.} so as they (although in themselves
dead\index{Death:spiritual, in sin ``f10!} in sin) are hereby made willing and able freely\index{Conversion:renewal of
the will ``f10!} to answer\index{Effectual call:enables person to:freely answer call ``f10!} his call, and to accept
and embrace the grace\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} offered and\index{Effectual call:enables person
to:embrace grace ``f10!} conveyed therein.\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!};
Philippians 2:13\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 30:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  30, v.  
6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 68 \textit{Are the elect}\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}\textit{ only effectually called}\index{Effectual
call:calling ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. All the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!}, and they only, are effectually called\index{Effectual call:calling
``f10!};\footnote{\ Acts 13:48\index{44 Acts:ch.  13, v.  48, pg. ``f30!}.} although others may be, and often are,
outwardly called\index{Preaching:outward call ``f10!} by the ministry of the word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word
``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 22:14\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and have some common
operations\index{Holy Spirit:operations:common ``f10!} of the Spirit;\footnote{\ Matthew 7:22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7,
v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 13:20-21\index{40 Matthew:ch.  13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:4-6\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   6, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.} who, for their wilful neglect\index{Unbelievers:wilful neglect and contempt of
grace ``f10!} and contempt of the\index{Contempt:for grace of Gospel ``f10!} grace offered to\index{Grace:opposed
``f10!} them, being justly left\index{Punishment:just:contempt of grace left in unbelief ``f10!} in their
unbelief\index{unbelief (misbelief) ``f10!}, do never truly\index{Unbelievers:non-elect never truly come to Jesus
``f10!} come to Jesus Christ.\footnote{\ John 6:64-65\index{43 John:ch.   6, v.  64-65, pg. ``f30!}; John
12:38-40\index{43 John:ch.  12, v.  38-40, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 18:25\index{44 Acts:ch.  18, v.  25, pg.
``f30!}{}-27\index{44 Acts:ch.  18, v.  25-27, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 81:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}{}-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  81, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 69 \textit{What is the communion in grace}\index{Communion:in grace ``f10!}\textit{ which the members of
the}\index{Church members ``f10!}\textit{ invisible church}\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}\textit{ have with Christ?}

A. The communion in grace\index{Communion:in grace ``f10!} which the members of the\index{Church members ``f10!}
invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} have with Christ, is their partaking of the
virtue\index{Jesus:vicarious atonement ``f10!} of his mediation\index{Jesus:mediator:of covenant ``f10!}, in their
