``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} adoption\index{Adoption:in salvation
``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}
sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}, and whatever else, in this life, manifests their union
with\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} him.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 1:30\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
1, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 70 \textit{What is justification}\index{Justification:justification ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!} is an act of God's free grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}
unto sinners,\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2, 24-25\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v. 
22, 24-25, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 4:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} in which he
pardons\index{Justification:pardoned of sin ``f10!} all their sins, accepts and\index{Justification:accepted by God as
righteous ``f10!} accounts\index{Justification:accounted by God as righteous ``f10!} their persons righteous
in\index{Jesus:righteousness imputed to believers ``f10!} his sight;\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:19\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}, 21\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  19, 21, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2-25, 27-28\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  22-25, 27-28, pg. ``f30!}.}
not for any thing wrought in them\index{Salvation:not by:works ``f10!}, or done by them,\footnote{\ Titus 3:5\index{56
Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}, 7\index{56 Titus:ch.   3, v.   5, 7, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:7\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} but only for the perfect obedience\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}
and full satisfaction of Christ\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice ``f10!}, by God imputed to\index{Imputation:of
Christ's righteousness by faith ``f10!} them,\footnote{\ Romans 4:6-8\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7-19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and
received by faith\index{Faith:instrument:of justification ``f10!} alone.\footnote{\ Acts 10:43\index{44 Acts:ch.  10,
v.  43, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:9\index{50
Philippians:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 71 \textit{How is justification}\index{Justification:justification ``f10!}\textit{ an act of God's free
grace}\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Although Christ, by his obedience and death, did\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} make a proper, real, and full
satisfaction to God's\index{Jesus:satisfied divine justice ``f10!} justice in the behalf of them that are
justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 5:8-10, 19\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   8-10, 19,
pg. ``f30!}.} yet inasmuch as God accepts the\index{Believers:accepted in Christ ``f10!} satisfaction from a
surety\index{Jesus:surety for the elect ``f10!}, which he might have demanded of them, and did provide this surety, his
own only Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 2:5-6\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   5-6, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 7:22\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}0\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 20:28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  20, v.  28, pg. ``f30!};
Daniel 9:24, 26\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.  24, 26, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 53:4-6, 10-12\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  53, v.  
4-6, 10-12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  32, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  18-19, pg.
``f30!}.} imputing\index{Imputation:of Christ's righteousness by faith ``f10!} his
righteousness\index{Jesus:righteousness imputed to believers ``f10!} to them,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 5:21\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   5, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and requiring\index{Salvation:faith alone required ``f10!} nothing of them
for their justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!} but faith\index{Faith:instrument:of justification
``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24, pg.
``f30!}{}-25\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} which also is his gift,\index{Justification:free gift
``f10!}\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} their justification is to them of
free grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 72 \textit{What is justifying}\index{Justification:by faith ``f10!}\textit{ faith?}

A. Justifying\index{Justification:by faith ``f10!} faith is a saving grace\index{Grace:of salvation
``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 10:39\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  39, pg. ``f30!}.} wrought in the heart of
a\index{Heart:new:grace applied ``f10!} sinner by the Spirit\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit ``f10!}\footnote{\ 2
Corinthians 4:13\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}7-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and word of God,\footnote{\ Romans 10:1\index{45
Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 17\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14,
17, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby he, being convinced\index{Repentance:conviction of sin, misery, and disability ``f10!} of his
sin and misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!}, and of the disability in\index{Sin:original:utterly unable and
unwilling to do will of God ``f10!} himself and all other creatures\index{creatures ``f10!} to recover
him\index{Justification:recovery from lost condition ``f10!} out of his lost condition\index{Mankind:lost condition
``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 2:37\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 4:12\index{44 Acts:ch.   4, v.  12, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 16:30\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; John 16:8-9\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.   8-9, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 5:6\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}.} not only assents\index{Justification:faith assents to truth of Gospel ``f10!} to the truth of\index{God's
attributes:truth ``f10!} the promise of the\index{Gospel:promise ``f10!} gospel\index{Gospel:gospel
``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13,
pg. ``f30!}.} but receives\index{Faith:instrument:for receiving Christ ``f10!} and rests\index{Faith:resting on Christ
``f10!} upon Christ and his righteousness\index{Jesus:righteousness imputed to believers ``f10!}, therein held forth,
for pardon of sin\index{Justification:pardoned of sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}2\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 10:43\index{44 Acts:ch.  10, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
16:31\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  31, pg. ``f30!}.} and for the accepting and\index{Justification:accepted by God as
righteous ``f10!} accounting of\index{Justification:accounted by God as righteous ``f10!} his person righteous in the
sight of God for salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Philippians 3:9\index{50
Philippians:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 15:11\index{44 Acts:ch.  15, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 73 \textit{How does faith}\index{Faith:instrument:of justification ``f10!}\textit{ justify a}\index{Justification:by
faith ``f10!}\textit{ sinner in the sight of God?}

A. Faith\index{Faith:saving ``f10!} justifies a\index{Justification:by faith ``f10!} sinner in the sight of God, not
because of those other graces\index{Faith:accompanied by graces ``f10!} which do always accompany it, or of good
works\index{Good works:adorn profession of faith ``f10!} that are the fruits\index{Good works:fruit of salvation
``f10!} of it,\footnote{\ Galatians 3:11\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 3:2\index{45
Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} nor as if the grace of
faith\index{Faith:given by grace ``f10!}, or any act thereof, were imputed to\index{Imputation:of Christ's
righteousness by faith ``f10!} him for his justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans
4:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45
Romans:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} but only as it is an instrument\index{Faith:instrument:of justification ``f10!}
by which he receives\index{Faith:instrument:for receiving Christ ``f10!} and applies\index{Faith:instrument:which
applies Christ to believers ``f10!} Christ and his righteousness\index{Jesus:righteousness imputed to believers
``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!};
Philippians 3:9\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 74 \textit{What is adoption}\index{Adoption:in salvation ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Adoption\index{Adoption:in salvation ``f10!} is an act of the free grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} of
God,\footnote{\ 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} in and for his only Son\index{Jesus:Son of
God ``f10!} Jesus Christ,\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
4:4\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby all
those that are justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!} are received into the number of his
children,\footnote{\ John 1:1\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{43 John:ch.   1, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}
have his name put upon them,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 4:18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   4, v.  18, pg. ``f30!};
Revelation 3:1\index{66 Revelation:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{66 Revelation:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} the
Spirit of his\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ ``f10!} Son given to them,\footnote{\ Galatians 4:6\index{48
Galatians:ch.   4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} are under his fatherly\index{Father:God the ``f10!} care and
dispensations\index{Adoption:fatherly dispensations ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 103:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}3\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 14:26\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  14, v.  26, pg.
``f30!}; Matthew 6:32\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.} admitted to all the liberties\index{Christian
liberty:privileges of children of God ``f10!} and privileges\index{Believers:privileges ``f10!} of the sons of God,
made heirs\index{Believers:heirs (salvation, promises, glory) ``f10!} of all the promises, and fellow heirs with Christ
in glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:with Christ ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Hebrews 6:12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6,
v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}7\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 75 \textit{What is sanctification}\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} is a work of God's grace\index{Grace:of salvation ``f10!},
whereby they whom God has, before the foundation\index{Predestination:before foundation of world. ``f10!} of the world,
chosen\index{Election:chosen by God ``f10!} to be holy\index{Believers:holy:chosen to be ``f10!}, are in time, through
the powerful operation\index{Holy Spirit:operations:saving ``f10!} of his Spirit\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:4\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 6:11\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Thessalonians 2:13\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} applying the death\index{Jesus:death:death
``f10!} and resurrection of Christ\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!} unto them,\footnote{\ Romans
6:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-6\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.} renewed
in\index{Sanctification:renewed in image of God ``f10!} their whole man after the image\index{Mankind:image of God
``f10!} of God;\footnote{\ Ephesians 4:23-24\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} having the seeds of
repentance unto\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!} life, and all other saving graces, put into their
hearts\index{Heart:new:grace applied ``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 11:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  11, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John
3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} and those graces\index{Grace:in believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} so
stirred up, increased, and strengthened,\index{Sanctification:supply of strength from Holy Spirit
``f10!}\footnote{\ Jude 1:20\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v. 
11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 3:16\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v. 
16-19, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:10-11\index{51 Colossians:ch.   1, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} as that they more and more
die unto\index{Sanctification:die unto sin ``f10!} sin, and rise unto\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:in newness
of life ``f10!} newness of life.\footnote{\ Romans 6:4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 76 \textit{What is repentance unto}\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!}\textit{ life?}

A. Repentance\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!} unto life is a saving grace\index{Grace:of salvation
``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 2:2\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  25,
pg. ``f30!}.} wrought in the heart of a\index{Heart:new:grace applied ``f10!} sinner by the
Spirit\index{Revelation:Word and Spirit ``f10!}\footnote{\ Zechariah 12:10\index{38 Zechariah:ch.  12, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}.} and word of God,\footnote{\ Acts 11:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  11, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}, 20-21\index{44 Acts:ch. 
11, v.  18, 20-21, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby, out of the sight and sense, not only of the
danger\index{Repentance:apprehension of danger of sin ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ezekiel 18:28, 30, 32\index{26 Ezekiel:ch. 
18, v.  28, 30, 32, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 15:17-18\index{42 Luke:ch.  15, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}; Hosea 2:6-7\index{28
Hosea:ch.   2, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} but also of the filthiness\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} and
odiousness\index{Sin:odious before God ``f10!} of his sins,\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:31\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  31,
pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 30:22\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  30, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} and upon the
apprehension\index{Repentance:apprehension of God's mercy ``f10!} of God's mercy in\index{God's attributes:merciful
``f10!} Christ to such as are penitent\index{Repentance:penitence ``f10!},\footnote{\ Joel 2:12\index{29 Joel:ch.   2,
v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  12-13, pg. ``f30!}.} he so grieves for\index{Sin:grief and hatred
of ``f10!}\footnote{\ Jeremiah 31:18\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v. 
18-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and hates\index{Sin:to be hated ``f10!} his sins,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} as that he
turns\index{Repentance:forsaking sin ``f10!} from them all to God,\footnote{\ Acts 26:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  26, v.  18,
pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 14:6\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  14, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Kings 8:47-48\index{11 1 Kings:ch.   8, v. 
47-48, pg. ``f30!}.} purposing\index{Repentance:purposing to walk with God ``f10!} and endeavoring\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:endeavoring ``f10!} constantly\index{Believers:desire to obey God ``f10!} to walk with
him\index{Believers:obedience:strive for new ``f10!} in all the ways of new obedience.\footnote{\ Psalm 119:6, 59,
128\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   6, 59, 128, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 1:6\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Kings
23:25\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  23, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 77 \textit{Wherein do justification}\index{Justification:justification ``f10!}\textit{ and
sanctification}\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}\textit{ differ?}

A. Although sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} be inseparably\index{Sanctification:inseparable
from:justification ``f10!} joined with justification\index{Justification:justification ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 1:30\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 6:11\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  
6, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} yet they differ, in that God in justification imputes\index{Imputation:of Christ's
righteousness by faith ``f10!} the righteousness of\index{Jesus:righteous ``f10!} Christ;\footnote{\ Romans 4:6,
8\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.   6, 8, pg. ``f30!}.} in sanctification his Spirit infuses grace\index{Grace:in
believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!}, and enables\index{Sanctification:enabled by:grace ``f10!} to the exercise
thereof;\footnote{\ Ezekiel 36:27\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.  36, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} in the former, sin is
pardoned;\index{Sanctification:pardoned of sin ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} in the
other, it is subdued\index{Sanctification:sin subdued ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Romans 6:6, 14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.  
6, 14, pg. ``f30!}.} the one does equally free all believers\index{Justification:frees all believers from wrath of God
``f10!} from the revenging\index{Revenge:God's ``f10!} wrath of God\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}, and that
perfectly in this life, that they never fall\index{Assurance:never fall from being saved ``f10!} into
condemnation\index{Believers:never fall into condemnation ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  
3, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}{}-34\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  33-34, pg. ``f30!}.} the
other is neither equal in all\index{Sanctification:not equal in all ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 2:12-14\index{62 1
John:ch.   2, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 5:12-14\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   5, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}.} nor in this
life perfect in any,\footnote{\ 1 John 1:8, 10\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   8, 10, pg. ``f30!}.} but growing
up\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:to perfection ``f10!} to perfection\index{Sanctification:growing to perfection
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:12\index{50
Philippians:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 78 \textit{Whence arises the imperfection of}\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!}\textit{
sanctification}\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}\textit{ in believers?}

A. The imperfection of\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!}
sanctification\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} in believers arises from the
remnants\index{Sanctification:remnants of corruption remain ``f10!} of sin abiding in every\index{Sin:remnants in
believers ``f10!} part of them, and the perpetual lustings\index{Sexual immorality:lust ``f10!} of the flesh against
the spirit\index{Sanctification:ongoing lusting of flesh against the spirit ``f10!}; whereby they are often foiled with
temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, and fall into many sins,\footnote{\ Romans 7:18\index{45 Romans:ch.  
7, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  18, 23, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 14:66-72\index{41 Mark:ch.  14, v. 
66-72, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:11-12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.} are hindered in all their
spiritual services\index{Good works:spiritual services ``f10!},\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}.} and their best works are imperfect and\index{Good works:mixed with weakness and imperfection ``f10!}
defiled in the sight of God.\footnote{\ Isaiah 64:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  64, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 28:38\index{02
Exodus:ch.  28, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 79 \textit{May not true believers}\index{Believers:cannot fall from state of grace ``f10!}\textit{, by reason of
their imperfections}\index{Sanctification:imperfection in believers ``f10!}\textit{, and the many
temptations}\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}\textit{ and sins they are overtaken}\index{Perseverance:not overtaken
by temptation and sin ``f10!}\textit{ with, fall away from the state of grace}\index{Grace:state:fall from
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. True believers, by\index{Assurance:of salvation ``f10!} reason of the unchangeable\index{God's
attributes:unchangeable ``f10!} love of God\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Jeremiah 31:3\index{24
Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and his decree\index{Predestination:eternal decrees ``f10!} and covenant
to\index{Covenant:promises ``f10!} give them perseverance\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!},\footnote{\ 2
Timothy 2:19\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  19-21, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Samuel 23:5\index{10 2 Samuel:ch.  23, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} their inseparable\index{Believers:union with
Christ:inseparable ``f10!} union with\index{Believers:union with Christ:mystical ``f10!} Christ,\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 1:8-9\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.} his continual intercession\index{Jesus:in
heaven:intercession made for all believers ``f10!} for them,\footnote{\ Hebrews 7:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   7, v.  25,
pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}.} and the Spirit and seed of
God\index{Believers:seed of God planted within ``f10!} abiding in them\index{Holy Spirit:abiding in believers
``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 2:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.  27, pg.
``f30!}; 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} can neither totally\index{Assurance:never fall from
being saved ``f10!} nor finally fall away from the state of grace\index{Grace:state:fall from
``f10!},\footnote{\ Jeremiah 32:40\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  32, v.  40, pg. ``f30!}; John 10:28\index{43 John:ch.  10, v.
28, pg. ``f30!}.} but are kept by the power\index{Perseverance:kept by God's power ``f10!} of God through faith
unto\index{Faith:saving ``f10!} salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter
1:5\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 80 \textit{Can true believers}\index{Assurance:believer may not have at all times ``f10!}\textit{ be infallibly
assured that}\index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!}\textit{ they are in the estate of grace}\index{Grace:estate of
``f10!}\textit{, and that they shall persevere}\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!}\textit{ therein unto
salvation}\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Such as truly\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!} believe in Christ, and endeavor to walk in
all\index{Believers:strive to walk in good conscience ``f10!} good conscience\index{Conscience:good, endeavour for
``f10!} before him,\footnote{\ 1 John 2:3\index{62 1 John:ch.   2, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} may, without extraordinary
revelation\index{Revelation:extraordinary ``f10!}, by faith grounded\index{Faith:grounded on God's promises ``f10!}
upon the truth\index{God's attributes:truth ``f10!} of God's promises\index{Assurance:promises of God ``f10!}, and by
the Spirit enabling the\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!}m\index{Assurance:enabled
by Holy Spirit ``f10!} to discern in\index{Grace:discern in self ``f10!} themselves those graces\index{Grace:in
believers:by Holy Spirit ``f10!} to which the promises\index{Salvation:promises made ``f10!} of life are
made,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 2:12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.
3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}, 18-19, 21, 24\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.  14,
18-19, 21, 24, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 4:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.  13,
pg. ``f30!}, 16\index{62 1 John:ch.   4, v.  13, 16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 6:11-12\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   6, v.  11-12,
pg. ``f30!}.} and bearing witness with\index{Assurance:Holy Spirit witnesses with our spirits ``f10!} their
spirits\index{Conversion:Holy Spirit:bears witness to our spirits ``f10!} that they are the children of
God,\footnote{\ Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}
be infallibly assured that\index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!} they are in the estate of grace\index{Grace:estate
of ``f10!}, and shall persevere\index{Perseverance:of the saints ``f10!} therein unto salvation.\footnote{\ 1 John
5:13\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 81 \textit{Are all true believers}\index{Assurance:believer may not have at all times ``f10!}\textit{ at all times
assured of}\index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!}\textit{ their present being in the estate of
grace}\index{Grace:estate of ``f10!}\textit{, and that they shall be saved}\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Assurance\index{Assurance:of state of grace ``f10!} of grace and salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith
``f10!} not being of the essence of faith\index{Faith:essence of ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 1:1\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   1, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}.} true believers may wait
long\index{Assurance:believer may await ``f10!} before they obtain it;\footnote{\ Isaiah 50:10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  50,
v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 88:1-18\index{19 Psalms:ch.  88, v.   1-18, pg. ``f30!}.} and, after the
enjoyment\index{Assurance:enjoyment of ``f10!} thereof, may have it weakened\index{Assurance:weak ``f10!} and
intermitted\index{Assurance:believer may not have at all times ``f10!}, through manifold distempers, sins,
temptations\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, and desertions;\footnote{\ Psalm 22:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  22, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 31:22\index{19 Psalms:ch.  31, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 51:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, pg.
``f30!}, 12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   8, 12, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 77:1-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  77, v.   1-12, pg.
``f30!}; Song of Solomon 5:2-3, 6\index{22 Song of Solomon:ch.   5, v.   2-3, 6, pg. ``f30!}.} yet are they never left
without such a presence and support of the Spirit of God\index{Holy Spirit:God's Spirit ``f10!} as keeps them from
sinking into\index{Assurance:Holy Spirit keeps believer from utter despair ``f10!} utter despair\index{despair
``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 3:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Job 13:15\index{18 Job:ch.  13, v.  15,
pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 73:15\index{19 Psalms:ch.  73, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{19 Psalms:ch.  73, v.  15, 23, pg.
``f30!}; Isaiah 54:7-10\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  54, v.   7-10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 82 \textit{What is the communion in glory}\index{Communion:in glory ``f10!}\textit{ which the members of
the}\index{Church members ``f10!}\textit{ invisible church}\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}\textit{ have with Christ?}

A. The communion in glory\index{Communion:in glory ``f10!} which the members of the\index{Church members ``f10!}
invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} have with Christ, is in this life,\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians
3:18\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.} immediately after death\index{Death:believers:immediate
perfection ``f10!},\footnote{\ Luke 23:43\index{42 Luke:ch.  23, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}.} and at last perfected
at\index{Resurrection:believers:perfected ``f10!} the resurrection and day of judgment\index{Judgement
day:believers:perfected ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 4:17\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  17, pg.
``f30!}.}

Q. 83 \textit{What is the communion in glory}\index{Communion:in glory ``f10!}\textit{ with Christ which the members of
the}\index{Church members ``f10!}\textit{ invisible church}\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}\textit{ enjoy
in}\index{Believers:enjoy:communion with God ``f10!}\textit{ this life?}

A. The members of the\index{Church members ``f10!} invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} have communicated to
them in this life the firstfruits of glory\index{Church:communicates firstfruits of glory with Christ ``f10!} with
Christ, as they are members of him their head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!}, and so in him are
interested\index{Believers:interest (share) in Christ ``f10!} in that glory\index{Jesus:glory ``f10!} which he is fully
possessed of;\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:5\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} and, as an
earnest\index{Believers:inheritance:earnest of ``f10!} thereof, enjoy the\index{Believers:enjoy:sense of God's love
``f10!} sense of God's love\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 5:5\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   5,
pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 1:22\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.} peace of
conscience\index{Conscience:peace of ``f10!}, joy in\index{Joy:in Holy Spirit ``f10!} the Holy Ghost\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!}, and hope of glory\index{Hope:of glory ``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  
5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 14:17\index{45 Romans:ch.  14, v. 
17, pg. ``f30!}.} as, on the contrary, sense of God's revenging\index{Revenge:God's ``f10!} wrath, horror of
conscience\index{Conscience:horror of ``f10!}, and a fearful\index{Fear:of God:abject ``f10!}
expectation\index{Judgement day:fearful expectation ``f10!} of judgment, are\index{Judgement day:expectation ``f10!} to
the wicked the\index{Judgement day:wicked:fearful expectation ``f10!} beginning of their torments
which\index{Punishment:everlasting:torments (body and soul) ``f10!} they shall endure after
death\index{Death:following:wicked endure torments ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 4:13\index{01 Genesis:ch.   4, v.  13,
pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 27:4\index{40 Matthew:ch.  27, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 10:27\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v. 
27, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 2:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Mark 9:44\index{41 Mark:ch.   9, v.  44, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 84 \textit{Shall all men die}\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Death being\index{Death:wages of sin ``f10!} threatened as\index{God's law:commandments:threatenings for disobedience
``f10!} the wages\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!} of sin,\footnote{\ Romans 6:23\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v. 
23, pg. ``f30!}.} it is appointed unto all men once to die;\footnote{\ Hebrews 9:27\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   9, v.  27,
pg. ``f30!}.} for that all have sinned\index{Sin:all have sinned ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 5:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  
5, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{45 Romans:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 85 \textit{Death, being}\index{Death:wages of sin ``f10!}\textit{ the wages}\index{Death:punishment for sin
``f10!}\textit{ of sin, why are not the righteous delivered from death, seeing}\index{Death:righteous not delivered
from temporal death ``f10!}\textit{ all their sins are forgiven}\index{Salvation:sins forgiven in Christ
``f10!}\textit{ in Christ?}

A. The righteous shall\index{Death:believers:delivered from sting of ``f10!} be delivered from death itself at the last
day\index{Last day:last day ``f10!}, and even in death are delivered from the sting and curse of it\index{Curse:of
death, delivered from ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:26, 55-57\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  26, 55-57, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} so
that, although they die, yet\index{Death:righteous not delivered from temporal death ``f10!} it is out of God's
love\index{God's attributes:love ``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah 57:1-2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  57, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; 2
Kings 22:20\index{12 2 Kings:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} to free them perfectly from sin and
misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!},\footnote{\ Revelation 14:13\index{66 Revelation:ch.  14, v.  13, pg. ``f30!};
Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.} and to
make them capable of further communion\index{Communion:with Christ ``f10!} with Christ in
glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:with Christ ``f10!}, which they then enter upon.\footnote{\ Luke
23:43\index{42 Luke:ch.  23, v.  43, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 1:23\index{50 Philippians:ch.   1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 86 \textit{What is the communion in glory}\index{Communion:in glory ``f10!}\textit{ with Christ, which the members of
the}\index{Church members ``f10!}\textit{ invisible church}\index{Church:invisible ``f10!}\textit{ enjoy immediately
after death}\index{Death:believers:immediate perfection ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The communion in glory\index{Communion:in glory ``f10!} with Christ, which the members of the\index{Church members
``f10!} invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} enjoy immediately after death\index{Death:believers:immediate
perfection ``f10!}, is, in that their souls are\index{Believers:souls made perfect at death ``f10!} then made perfect

2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} and received into the highest heavens,\footnote{\ 2
Corinthians 5:1, 6, 8\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   5, v.   1, 6, 8, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 1:23\index{50
Philippians:ch.   1, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 3:21\index{44 Acts:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:10\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.} where they behold\index{Believers:behold face of God in glory ``f10!} the face
of\index{Resurrection:believers:behold face of God ``f10!} God in light and glory\index{Resurrection:believers:into
glory:light ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 13:12\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} waiting for\index{Resurrection:believers:waiting expectantly ``f10!} the
full redemption\index{Redemption:full ``f10!} of their bodies,\index{Bodies in graves:believers
``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  23, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 16:9\index{19 Psalms:ch.  16, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.} which even in death
continue\index{Death:believers:continue united to Christ ``f10!} united to Christ\index{Believers:union with
Christ:mystical ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Thessalonians 4:14\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and
rest in their graves\index{Resurrection:bodies:await in graves ``f10!} as in their beds,\footnote{\ Isaiah
57:2\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  57, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} till at the last day\index{Last day:last day ``f10!} they be again
united to the\index{Jesus:human nature:united with divine ``f10!}ir\index{Resurrection:bodies:united to souls ``f10!}
souls.\footnote{\ Job 19:26-27\index{18 Job:ch.  19, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}.} Whereas the
souls\index{Punishment:hell:wicked cast into ``f10!} of the wicked are\index{Judgement day:wicked:cast into:hell
``f10!} at their death cast into hell\index{Hell:hell ``f10!}, where they remain in torments
and\index{Punishment:everlasting:torments (body and soul) ``f10!} utter darkness\index{darkness, spiritual ``f10!}, and
their bodies kept\index{Bodies in graves:unbelievers ``f10!} in their graves, as in their prisons, till the
resurrection\index{Resurrection:general, of dead ``f10!} and judgment of the\index{Judgement:final ``f10!} great
day.\footnote{\ Luke 16:23-24\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 1:25\index{44 Acts:ch.   1, v.  25,
pg. ``f30!}; Jude 1:6\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 87 \textit{What are we to believe concerning the resurrection}\index{Resurrection:general, of dead ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. We are to believe, that at the last day\index{Last day:last day ``f10!} there shall be a general
resurrection\index{Resurrection:general, of dead ``f10!} of the dead, both\index{Death:following:all men raised ``f10!}
of the just and unjust\index{Resurrection:of just and unjust ``f10!}:\footnote{\ Acts 24:15\index{44 Acts:ch.  24, v. 
15, pg. ``f30!}.} when they that are then found alive\index{Last day:those alive on earth ``f10!} shall in a moment
be\index{Resurrection:bodies:changed in a moment ``f10!} changed; and the selfsame bodies of the dead
which\index{Death:bodies:laid in graves ``f10!} were laid in the grave\index{Resurrection:bodies:await in graves
``f10!}, being then again united to the\index{Jesus:human nature:united with divine
``f10!}ir\index{Resurrection:bodies:united to souls ``f10!} souls forever, shall be raised up by the
power\index{Resurrection:believers:by the power of Christ ``f10!} of Christ.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:51-53\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  51-53, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 4:15-17\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  15-17, pg.
``f30!}; John 5:28-29\index{43 John:ch.   5, v.  28-29, pg. ``f30!}.} The bodies of the\index{Resurrection:bodies:same
ones as before death, for just and unjust ``f10!} just, by the Spirit of Christ\index{Holy Spirit:Spirit of Christ
``f10!}, and by virtue\index{Jesus:vicarious atonement ``f10!} of his resurrection\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the
dead ``f10!} as their head\index{Church:Christ as head ``f10!}, shall be raised in
power\index{Resurrection:believers:in power ``f10!}, spiritual,
incorruptible\index{Resurrection:believers:incorruptible ``f10!}, and made like to his glorious
body\index{Jesus:resurrection:body:glorious ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 15:21-23, 42-44\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  21-23, 42-44, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 3:21\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}.} and the bodies of the wicked shall\index{Resurrection:wicked raised in dishonour ``f10!} be raised up in
dishonor by him, as an offended judge\index{Judgement:final ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 5:27-29\index{43 John:ch.   5, v. 
27-29, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:33\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} 


\bigskip

Q. 88 \textit{What shall immediately follow after the resurrection}\index{Resurrection:general, of dead
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Immediately after the resurrection\index{Resurrection:general, of dead ``f10!} shall follow the general and final
judgment\index{Judgement:final ``f10!} of angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men;\footnote{\ 2 Peter 2:4\index{61 2
Peter:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Jude 1:6\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.  
6-7, pg. ``f30!}, 14-15\index{65 Jude:v.   1, v.   6-7, 14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 25:46\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v. 
46, pg. ``f30!}.} the day and hour whereof no man knows, that\index{Jesus:return:no one knows hour ``f10!} all may
watch and\index{Jesus:return:watchfulness ``f10!} pray, and be\index{Prayer:in watchfulness for coming of the Lord
``f10!} ever ready for the coming of the Lord.\footnote{\ Matthew 24:36\index{40 Matthew:ch.  24, v.  36, pg. ``f30!},
42, 44\index{40 Matthew:ch.  24, v.  36, 42, 44, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 21:35-36\index{42 Luke:ch.  21, v.  35-36, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 89 \textit{What shall be done to the wicked at}\index{Judgement day:wicked:cast into:hell ``f10!}\textit{ the day of
judgment}\index{Judgement day:believers:perfected ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. At the day of judgment\index{Judgement day:believers:perfected ``f10!}, the wicked shall be set\index{Judgement
day:wicked:set on left ``f10!} on Christ's left hand,\footnote{\ Matthew 25:33\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  33, pg.
``f30!}.} and, upon clear evidence, and full conviction\index{Judgement day:wicked:full conviction of consciences
``f10!} of their own consciences,\footnote{\ Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45
Romans:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-16\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}.} shall have the
fearful\index{Fear:of God:abject ``f10!} but just sentence\index{Punishment:just:sentence ``f10!} of
condemnation\index{Punishment:condemnation ``f10!} pronounced against them;\footnote{\ Matthew 25:41\index{40
Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}{}-43\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41-43, pg. ``f30!}.} and thereupon shall be
cast out\index{Punishment:hell:wicked cast into ``f10!} from the favorable presence of God, and the
glorious\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:fellowship ``f10!} fellowship with\index{Fellowship:with Christ
``f10!} Christ, his saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!}, and all his holy\index{Angels:holy ``f10!}
angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!}, into hell\index{Hell:hell ``f10!}, to be
punished\index{Punishment:everlasting:torments (body and soul) ``f10!} with unspeakable torments, both of body and
soul, with the devil\index{Devil:devil ``f10!} and his angels forever.\footnote{\ Luke 16:26\index{42 Luke:ch.  16, v. 
26, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 1:8-9\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 90 \textit{What shall be done to the righteous at}\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:with Christ
``f10!}\textit{ the day of judgment}\index{Judgement day:believers:perfected ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. At the day of judgment\index{Judgement day:believers:perfected ``f10!}, the righteous, being
caught\index{Resurrection:believers:into glory:with Christ ``f10!} up to Christ in the clouds,\footnote{\ 1
Thessalonians 4:17\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} shall be set on his right hand, and there
openly acknowledged\index{Judgement day:believers:acknowledged by God ``f10!} and acquitted\index{Judgement
day:believers:acquitted by God ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 10:32\index{40 Matthew:ch.  10, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
25:33\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  33, pg. ``f30!}.} shall join with him in the judging of
reprobate\index{Judgement:of reprobate angels and men ``f10!} angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} and men,\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 6:2-3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   6, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.} and shall be received into
heaven\index{Believers:received into heaven ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 25:34, 46\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  34, 46,
pg. ``f30!}.} where they shall be fully and forever freed from all\index{Resurrection:believers:freed from sin ``f10!}
sin and misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!};\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}7\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 14:13\index{66 Revelation:ch.  14, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}.} filled with inconceivable joys\index{Joy:inconceivable ``f10!},\footnote{\ Psalm 16:11\index{19 Psalms:ch. 
16, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} made perfectly holy\index{Believers:holy:made perfect at death ``f10!} and
happy\index{happiness ``f10!} both in body and soul, in\index{Believers:souls made perfect at death ``f10!} the company
of innumerable\index{Heaven:innumerable saints and angels ``f10!} saints\index{Believers:saints ``f10!} and holy
angels,\footnote{\ Hebrews 12:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}{}-23\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} but especially in the immediate
vision\index{Resurrection:believers:immediate vision of God ``f10!} and fruition of God the Father\index{Father:God the
``f10!}, of our Lord Jesus Christ, and of the Holy Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!}, to all
eternity\index{Believers:blessed to all eternity ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 13:12\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  13, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 4:17\index{52 1
Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-18\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}.} And this is
the perfect and full communion, which\index{Communion:with God ``f10!} the members of the\index{Church members ``f10!}
invisible church\index{Church:invisible ``f10!} shall enjoy with Christ in glory, at the resurrection and day of
judgment.


\bigskip

Q. 91 \textit{What is the duty which God}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{ requires
of man?}

A. The duty which God\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} requires of man, is obedience to his
revealed will\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 12:1-2\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.   1-2, pg.
``f30!}; Micah 6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 15:22\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.  15, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 92 \textit{What did God at first reveal unto}\index{God's law:commandments:first revelation ``f10!}\textit{ man as
the rule of his}\index{God's law:moral:rule for obedience ``f10!}\textit{ obedience?}

A. The rule of obedience\index{Covenant:works:perfect obedience required ``f10!} revealed to\index{Revelation:God's law
``f10!} Adam in the\index{Adam:given a law ``f10!} estate of innocence\index{Mankind:created:state of innocence
``f10!}, and to all mankind in\index{God's law:God's will for mankind ``f10!} him, besides a special command not to eat
of the fruit of the tree of the\index{Tree:of the knowledge of good and evil ``f10!} knowledge of good and evil, was
the moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law.\footnote{\ Genesis 1:2\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-27\index{01 Genesis:ch.   1, v.  26-27, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis
2:17\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 93 \textit{What is the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law?}

A. The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law is the declaration\index{God's law:moral:declaration of
God's will ``f10!} of the will of God to mankind\index{God's law:God's will for mankind ``f10!}, directing and binding
everyone\index{God's law:binding on all men ``f10!} to personal, perfect, and perpetual conformity\index{God's
law:moral:perpetual conformity required ``f10!} and obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!}
thereunto, in the frame and\index{God's law:commandments:address words, works, gestures ``f10!} disposition of the
whole man, soul\index{God's law:binding on whole man, soul and body ``f10!} and body,\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 5:1-3, 31,
33\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.   1-3, 31, 33, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 10:26-27\index{42 Luke:ch.  10, v.  26-27, pg.
``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 5:23\index{52 1
Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}.} and in performance of all those duties\index{God's
law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} of holiness\index{Believers:holy:being perfected ``f10!} and
righteousness which\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!} he owes to God and man:\footnote{\ Luke
1:75\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  75, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 14:16\index{44 Acts:ch.  14, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} promising
life\index{God's law:commandments:promises included ``f10!} upon the fulfilling, and\index{Covenant:works:conditional
on perfect obedience ``f10!} threatening death\index{Death:punishment for sin ``f10!} upon the breach of it\index{God's
law:breach:death threatened ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}, 12\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, 12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 94 \textit{Is there any use of the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law to man since the
fall}\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Although no man, since the fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, can attain to
righteousness\index{God's law:moral:no person attain righteousness ``f10!} and life by the moral\index{God's
law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law;\footnote{\ Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians
2:16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} yet there is great use thereof, as well common to all men, as
peculiar either to the unregenerate\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate ``f10!}, or the
regenerate\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 1:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   8, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 95 \textit{Of what use is the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law to all men?}

A. The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law is of use to all men, to inform them of the holy\index{God's
attributes:holy:nature ``f10!} nature and will of God,\footnote{\ Leviticus 11:44-45\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  11, v. 
44-45, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 20:7-8\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  20, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:12\index{45 Romans:ch.
7, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} and of their duty, binding them\index{God's law:binding on all men ``f10!} to walk
accordingly;\footnote{\ Micah 6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.   2, v. 
10, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} to convince them\index{God's law:convince men of
disability to keep ``f10!} of their disability to keep it, and of the sinful pollution\index{Sin:original:corrupt
nature:polluted ``f10!} of their nature, hearts, and lives\index{Heart:polluted ``f10!};\footnote{\ Psalm
19:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}{}-12\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:7\index{45
Romans:ch.   7, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} to humble them\index{Humility:before God ``f10!} in the sense of their sin and
misery\index{Punishment:misery ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 3:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}, 23\index{45
Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, 23, pg. ``f30!}.} and thereby help them\index{God's law:provides sight of need for Christ
``f10!} to a clearer sight of the need they have of Christ,\footnote{\ Galatians 3:21\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v. 
21, pg. ``f30!}{}-22\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} and of the perfection of
his\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!} obedience.\footnote{\ Romans 10:4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 96 \textit{What particular use is there of the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law to
unregenerate}\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate ``f10!}\textit{ men?}

A. The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law is of use to unregenerate\index{Unbelievers:unregenerate
``f10!} men, to awaken\index{God's law:awaken conscience ``f10!} their consciences to\index{Conscience:awakened ``f10!}
flee\index{Wrath:of God:flee from ``f10!} from wrath to\index{Wrath:of God:pending ``f10!} come,\footnote{\ 1 Timothy
1:9-10\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}.} and to drive\index{God's law:drive men to Christ ``f10!}
them to Christ;\footnote{\ Galatians 3:24\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} or, upon their continuance
in the estate and\index{Unbelievers:in estate and way of sin ``f10!} way of sin, to leave them
inexcusable\index{Unbelievers:inexcusable ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 1:20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  20, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} and under the
curse thereof\index{Curse:of the law ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 97 \textit{What special use is there of the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law to the
regenerate}\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Although they that are regenerate\index{Regeneration:regeneration ``f10!}, and believe in Christ, be
delivered\index{Covenant:works:believers delivered from ``f10!} from the moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral
``f10!} law as a covenant of works\index{Covenant:works:works ``f10!},\footnote{\ Romans 6:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   6,
v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 7:4, 6\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.   4, 6, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 4:4\index{48
Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{48 Galatians:ch.   4, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} so as thereby they are
neither justified\index{Justification:justified ``f10!}\footnote{\ Romans 3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} nor condemned;\footnote{\ Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch. 
5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}.} yet, besides the general uses thereof common to them with all men, it is of special use, to show them how
much they are bound to Christ for his fulfilling it\index{Jesus:obedience:to God's law ``f10!}, and enduring the curse
thereof in\index{Jesus:curse in believers' stead ``f10!} their stead\index{Jesus:vicarious atonement ``f10!}, and for
their good;\footnote{\ Romans 7:24-25\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:3\index{45 Romans:ch.  
8, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:13\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3,
v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} and thereby to
provoke\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!} them to more thankfulness,\footnote{\ Luke 1:6\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.   6,
pg. ``f30!}8-69, 74-75\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  68-69, 74-75, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 1:12-14\index{51 Colossians:ch.
1, v.  12-14, pg. ``f30!}.} and to express the same in their greater care to conform\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} themselves thereunto as the rule of their obedience.\footnote{\ Romans
7:22\index{45 Romans:ch.   7, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 12:2\index{45 Romans:ch.  12, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Titus
2:11-14\index{56 Titus:ch.   2, v.  11-14, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 98 \textit{Where is the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law summarily
comprehended}\index{God's law:moral:summarily comprehended in ten commandments ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law is summarily comprehended\index{God's law:moral:summarily
comprehended in ten commandments ``f10!} in the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} commandments, which were
delivered by\index{God's law:commandments:delivered on Sinai ``f10!} the voice of God\index{God's
law:commandments:delivered by voice of God ``f10!} upon mount Sinai\index{Sinai, mount ``f10!}, and written by him in
two tables\index{God's law:commandments:two tables ``f10!} of stone;\index{God's law:commandments:tablets of stone
``f10!}\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 10:4\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  10, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 34:1\index{02 Exodus:ch. 
34, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}.} and are recorded in the twentieth chapter
of Exodus. The four first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}s\index{God's law:commandments:first
four, duty to God ``f10!} containing our duty to God\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}, and
the other six\index{Sabbath:six days:for own affairs ``f10!} our duty to man\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to
others ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 22:37-38, 40\index{40 Matthew:ch.  22, v.  37-38, 40, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 99 \textit{What rules are to be observed for the}\index{God's law:commandments:rules for right understanding
``f10!}\textit{ right understanding of the ten}\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ commandments?}

A. For the right understanding\index{God's law:commandments:rules for right understanding ``f10!} of the ten\index{God's
law:commandments:ten ``f10!} commandments, these rules are to be observed: 1. That the law is perfect, and binds
everyone\index{God's law:binding on all men ``f10!} to full conformity in the whole man unto the righteousness
thereof\index{God's law:righteous requirements ``f10!}, and unto entire obedience\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} forever; so as to require the\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required
by God ``f10!} utmost perfection of every duty, and to\index{God's law:commandments:duties:perfection required ``f10!}
forbid the least degree\index{God's law:breach:least degree forbidden ``f10!} of every sin.\footnote{\ Psalm
19:7\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
5:21-22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}.} 2. That it is spiritual, and\index{God's law:spiritual
``f10!} so reaches the understanding, will, affections, and all\index{God's law:addresses affections ``f10!} other
powers of the soul; as\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:whole being ``f10!} well as words, works\index{God's
law:commandments:address words, works, gestures ``f10!}, and gestures.\footnote{\ Romans 7:14\index{45 Romans:ch.   7,
v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 6:5\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:21-22\index{40
Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}, 27-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-22, 27-28, pg. ``f30!}, 33-34, 37-39,
43-44\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-22, 27-28, 33-34, 37-39, 43-44, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 22:37-39\index{40
Matthew:ch.  22, v.  37-39, pg. ``f30!}.} 3. That one and the same thing, in divers respects, is required or
forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!} in several commandments\index{God's
law:commandments:multiple may apply ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Colossians 3:5\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}; Amos 8:5\index{30 Amos:ch.   8, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 1:19\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   1, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.  10, pg.
``f30!}.} 4. That as, where a duty is commanded\index{God's law:commandments:prohibitions and duties ``f10!}, the
contrary sin is forbidden;\footnote{\ Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy
6:13\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 4:9-10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.   9-10, pg.
``f30!}; Matthew 15:4-6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.} and, where a sin is forbidden, the contrary
duty is commanded:\footnote{\ Matthew 5:21-25\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-25, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:28\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}.} so, where a promise is\index{God's law:commandments:promises included ``f10!}
annexed, the contrary threatening is\index{God's law:commandments:threat and promise ``f10!}
included;\footnote{\ Exodus 20:12\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs 30:17\index{20 Proverbs:ch. 
30, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.} and, where a threatening is annexed, the contrary promise is included.\footnote{\ Jeremiah
18:7-8\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  18, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 20:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 15:1, 4-5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  15, v.   1, 4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 24:4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  24, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}{}-5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  24, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}.} 5. That what God forbids, is at no time to be
done;\footnote{\ Job 13:7\index{18 Job:ch.  13, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Job 36:21\index{18 Job:ch.  36, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 3:8\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 11:25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  11, v.  25, pg.
``f30!}.}[8] What he commands, is always our duty;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:8-9\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.   8-9,
pg. ``f30!}.} and yet every particular duty is not\index{God's law:commandments:duties:not at all times ``f10!} to be
done at all times.\footnote{\ Matthew 12:7\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} 6. That under one sin or
duty, all of the same kind are forbidden or commanded; together with all the causes, means, occasions, and appearances
thereof, and provocations thereunto.\footnote{\ Matthew 5:21-22\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!},
27-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.   5, v.  21-22, 27-28, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 15:4-6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   4-6, pg.
``f30!}; Hebrews 10:24-25\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  10, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 5:22-23\index{52 1
Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 5:2\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{48
Galatians:ch.   5, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:2\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{51
Colossians:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} 7. That what is forbidden or commanded to ourselves\index{God's
law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!}, we are bound, according to our places, to endeavor that\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:endeavoring ``f10!} it may be avoided or performed by others, according to the duty of their
places.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 19:17\index{03 Leviticus:ch. 
19, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Genesis 18:19\index{01 Genesis:ch.  18, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}; Joshua 24:15\index{06 Joshua:ch. 
24, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}{}-7\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.
6, v.   6-7, pg. ``f30!}.} 8. That in what is commanded to others, we are bound, according to our places and
calling\index{Calling:in life ``f10!}s, to be helpful to them;\footnote{\ 2 Corinthians 1:24\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.
1, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}.} and to take heed\index{God's law:commandments:duties:not what is forbidden ``f10!} of
partaking with others in: What is forbidden them.\footnote{\ 1 Timothy 5:22\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 100 \textit{What special things are we to consider in the ten}\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{
commandments?}

A. We are to consider, in the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} commandments, the preface, the\index{God's
law:commandments:preface ``f10!} substance of the commandment\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!}s
themselves, and several reasons annexed to some of them, the more to enforce them\index{God's law:commandments:words of
enforcement ``f10!}.


\bigskip

Q. 101 \textit{What is the preface to}\index{God's law:commandments:preface ``f10!}\textit{ the ten}\index{God's
law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ commandments?}

A. The preface to\index{God's law:commandments:preface ``f10!} the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}
commandments is contained in these words, I am the Lord thy God, which have brought you out of the land of
Egypt\index{Egypt ``f10!}, out of the house of bondage\index{bondage, slavery in Egypt ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus
20:2\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} Wherein God manifests his sovereignty\index{God's
attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!}, as being JEHOVAH\index{God's name:JEHOVAH ``f10!}, the eternal,\index{God's
attributes:eternal ``f10!} immutable\index{God's attributes:immutable ``f10!}, and almighty\index{God's
attributes:almighty power ``f10!} God;\footnote{\ Isaiah 44:6\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  44, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} having his
being in and of himself,\footnote{\ Exodus 3:14\index{02 Exodus:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} and giving being to all
his words\footnote{\ Exodus 6:3\index{02 Exodus:ch.   6, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.} and works\index{Providence:God's works
``f10!}:\footnote{\ Acts 17:24\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}, 28\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  24, 28, pg.
``f30!}.} and that he is a God in covenant, as\index{Covenant:administrations ``f10!} with Israel\index{Israel ``f10!}
of old, so with all his people;\footnote{\ Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
3:2\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} who, as he brought
them out of their bondage in Egypt, so he delivers us from our spiritual thraldom\index{Salvation:delivered from
thraldom to sin ``f10!};\footnote{\ Luke 1:74-75\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  74-75, pg. ``f30!}.} and that therefore we
are bound to take him for our God alone, and to keep all his commandments\index{God's
law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Peter 1:15-18\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   1, v.  15-18, pg.
``f30!}; Leviticus 18:30\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  18, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 19:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.
3, pg. ``f30!}7\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 102 \textit{What is the sum of the four commandments}\index{God's law:commandments:first four, duty to God
``f10!}\textit{ which contain our duty to God}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sum of the four commandments\index{God's law:commandments:first four, duty to God ``f10!} containing our duty to
God\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} is, to love the Lord\index{Love toward God:for God
``f10!} our God with all our heart, and with all our soul\index{Love toward God:with all our:soul ``f10!}, and with all
our strength\index{Love toward God:with all our:strength ``f10!}, and with all our mind.\footnote{\ Luke 10:27\index{42
Luke:ch.  10, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 103 \textit{Which is the first commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!} is, You shall have no other
gods\index{Idolatry:worshiping gods ``f10!} before me.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:3\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 104 \textit{What are the duties required}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{ in the
first commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The duties required\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} in the first commandment\index{God's
law:commandments:first ``f10!} are, the knowing and acknowledging of God\index{Worship:acknowledge God ``f10!} to be
the only true God, and our God;\footnote{\ 1 Chronicles 28:9\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  28, v.   9, pg. ``f30!};

Q. 105 \textit{What are the sins forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the first
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sins forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!} in the first commandment\index{God's

``f10!} not having a God;\footnote{\ Psalm 14:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  14, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 2:1\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}

gods\index{Idolatry:worshiping gods ``f10!} than one, or any with or instead of the true God;\footnote{\ Jeremiah
2:27-28\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   2, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 1:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.  
9, pg. ``f30!}.} the not having and avouching\index{Idolatry:not avouching God as God ``f10!} him for God, and our

``f10!} or neglect of anything\index{Worship:not to be:neglected ``f10!} due to him, required in this
commandment;\footnote{\ Isaiah 43:22-24\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  43, v.  22-24, pg. ``f30!}.} ignorance\index{ignorance
``f10!},\footnote{\ Jeremiah 4:2\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}2\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   4, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}; Hosea 4:1, 6\index{28 Hosea:ch.   4, v.   1, 6, pg. ``f30!}.} forgetfulness\index{Idolatry:forgetting God
``f10!},\footnote{\ Jeremiah 2:32\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.   2, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}} misapprehensions,\footnote{\ Acts
17:23\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}, 29\index{44 Acts:ch.  17, v.  23, 29, pg. ``f30!}.} false
opinions\index{Falsehood:false opinions ``f10!},\footnote{\ Isaiah 40:18\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  40, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}
unworthy and\index{Idolatry:unworthy and wicked thoughts about God ``f10!} wicked thoughts of\index{Idolatry:wicked
thoughts about God ``f10!} him;\footnote{\ Psalm 50:21\index{19 Psalms:ch.  50, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} bold and curious
searching\index{Providence:not to search into God's secrets ``f10!} into his secrets;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy
29:29\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  29, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}.} all profaneness\index{God's name:not to be:profaned
``f10!},\footnote{\ Titus 1:16\index{56 Titus:ch.   1, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 12:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  
1, pg. ``f30!}6\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  12, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} hatred of God\index{Sin:hatred of God
``f10!};\footnote{\ Romans 1:30\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  30, pg. ``f30!}.} self-love\index{self-love
``f10!},\footnote{\ 2 Timothy 3:2\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} self-seeking\index{self-seeking
``f10!},\footnote{\ Philippians 2:21\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.} and all other inordinate and
immoderate setting\index{Idolatry:immoderate setting of mind on other than God ``f10!} of our

things ``f10!} other things, and taking them off from him in whole or in part;\footnote{\ 1 John 2:15-16\index{62 1
