46\index{40 Matthew:ch.  25, v.  33-34, 46, pg. ``f30!}.} and made perfectly blessed in\index{Believers:blessed in/by
God ``f10!} the full enjoying of\index{Resurrection:believers:enjoy God ``f10!} God\footnote{\ Romans 8:2\index{45
Romans:ch.   8, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}9\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  29, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:2\index{62 1 John:ch.   3,
v.   2, pg. ``f30!}.} to all eternity\index{Believers:blessed to all eternity ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 16:11\index{19
Psalms:ch.  16, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 4:17\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 39 \textit{What is the duty which God}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{ requires
of man?}

A. The duty which God\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!} requires of man, is obedience to his
revealed will\index{Revelation:God's will ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 29:29\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  29, v.  29,
pg. ``f30!}; Micah 6:8\index{33 Micah:ch.   6, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 5:2-3\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.   2-3, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 40 \textit{What did God at first reveal to}\index{God's law:commandments:first revelation ``f10!}\textit{ man for the
rule of his}\index{God's law:moral:rule for obedience ``f10!}\textit{ obedience?}

A. The rule which\index{God's law:moral:rule for obedience ``f10!} God at first revealed to\index{Revelation:God's law
``f10!} man for his obedience, was the moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law.\footnote{\ Romans
2:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-15\index{45 Romans:ch.   2, v.  14-15, pg. ``f30!}; Romans
10:5\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 41 \textit{Wherein is the moral}\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!}\textit{ law summarily
comprehended}\index{God's law:moral:summarily comprehended in ten commandments ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The moral\index{God's law:commandments:moral ``f10!} law is summarily comprehended\index{God's law:moral:summarily
comprehended in ten commandments ``f10!} in the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}
commandments.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:13\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   4, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 19:17\index{40
Matthew:ch.  19, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  19, v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 42 \textit{What is the sum of the ten}\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ commandments?}

A. The sum of the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} commandments is, To love the Lord\index{Love toward
God:for God ``f10!} our God with all our heart, with all our soul\index{Love toward God:with all our:soul ``f10!}, with
all our strength\index{Love toward God:with all our:strength ``f10!}, and with all our mind; and our
neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!} as ourselves.\footnote{\ Matthew 22:37-40\index{40
Matthew:ch.  22, v.  37-40, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 43 \textit{What is the preface to}\index{God's law:commandments:preface ``f10!}\textit{ the ten}\index{God's
law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ commandments?}

A. The preface to\index{God's law:commandments:preface ``f10!} the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}
commandments is in these words, I am the Lord thy God, which have brought you out of the land of Egypt\index{Egypt
``f10!}, out of the house of bondage\index{bondage, slavery in Egypt ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:2\index{02
Exodus:ch.  20, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 44 \textit{What does }the\textit{ preface to}\index{God's law:commandments:preface ``f10!}\textit{ the
ten}\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ commandments teach us?}

A. The preface to\index{God's law:commandments:preface ``f10!} the ten\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}
commandments teaches us, That because God is the Lord, and our God, and Redeemer\index{Jesus:redeemer of God's elect
``f10!}, therefore we are bound to keep all his commandments\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Luke 1:74-75\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  74-75, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 1:14-19\index{60 1 Peter:ch.  
1, v.  14-19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 45 \textit{Which is the first commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!} is, You shalt have no other
gods\index{Idolatry:worshiping gods ``f10!} before me.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:3\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:7\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 46 \textit{What is required in the first commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!} requires us to know and acknowledge
God\index{Worship:acknowledge God ``f10!} to be the only true God, and our God; and to worship
and\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} glorify him accordingly.\footnote{\ 1 Chronicles 28:9\index{13 1
Chronicles:ch.  28, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 45:20-25\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  45, v.  20-25, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
4:10\index{40 Matthew:ch.   4, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 47 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the first
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!} forbids the denying,\index{Idolatry:denying the true
God ``f10!}\footnote{\ Psalm 14:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  14, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}.} or not worshipping and
glorifying\index{Worship:glorifying God ``f10!} the true God as God,\footnote{\ Romans 1:20\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.
20, pg. ``f30!}{}-21\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}.} and our God;\footnote{\ Psalm 81:10-11\index{19
Psalms:ch.  81, v.  10-11, pg. ``f30!}.} and the giving of that worship and glory to any\index{Idolatry:giving glory to
another than God ``f10!} other, which is due to him alone.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 8:16-18\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.   8, v. 
16-18, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:25\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 48 \textit{What are we specially taught by}\index{God's law:commandments:first, words 'before me' ``f10!}\textit{
these words, ``before me,'' in the first commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. These words, before me, in the first commandment\index{God's law:commandments:first ``f10!} teach us,
that\index{God's law:commandments:first, words 'before me' ``f10!} God, who sees all things, takes
notice\index{Idolatry:God takes special notice of this sin ``f10!} of, and is much displeased\index{Idolatry:displeases
God greatly ``f10!} with, the sin of having any other God.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 30:17-18\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch. 
30, v.  17-18, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 44:20-21\index{19 Psalms:ch.  44, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Ezekiel 8:12\index{26
Ezekiel:ch.   8, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 49 \textit{Which is the second commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The second commandment\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!} is, You shalt not make unto you any graven image,
or\index{Idolatry:graven image ``f10!} any likeness\index{Idolatry:worship of likeness of any created thing ``f10!} of
anything that is in heaven above, or that is in the earth beneath, or that is in the water under\index{Idolatry:bowing
to created entity ``f10!} the earth: you shalt not bow down thy self to them, nor serve the\index{Love toward God:in
service ``f10!}m\index{Idolatry:serve images ``f10!}: for I the Lord thy God am a jealous\index{God's
attributes:jealous ``f10!} God, visiting\index{Punishment:visiting iniquity ``f10!} the iniquity of the fathers upon
the children unto the third and\index{Punishment:to third and fourth generation ``f10!} fourth generation of them that
hate\index{Sin:hatred of God ``f10!} me; and showing mercy unto\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!} thousands of
them that love me\index{Love toward God:for God ``f10!}, and keep my commandments\index{God's law:commandments:ten
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:4-6\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:8-10\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.   8-10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 50 \textit{What is required in the second commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The second commandment\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!} requires the receiving, observing, and keeping
pure\index{Worship:to be observed and kept pure ``f10!} and entire, all such religious worship and ordinances
as\index{Worship:ordinances:to be:kept pure ``f10!} God has appointed in his Word\index{Scripture:word of
God:standard:for worship ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 12:32\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  12, v.  32, pg. ``f30!};
Matthew 28:20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 51 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the second
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The second commandment\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!} forbids the worshipping of\index{Worship:false:by
images ``f10!} God by images\index{Idolatry:images ``f10!},\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 4:15-19\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  
4, v.  15-19, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 1:22-23\index{45 Romans:ch.   1, v.  22-23, pg. ``f30!}.} or any other way not
appointed in his Word\index{Scripture:word of God:standard:for worship ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Leviticus 10:1-2\index{03
Leviticus:ch.  10, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}; Jeremiah 19:4-5\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  19, v.   4-5, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians
2:18\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-23\index{51 Colossians:ch.   2, v.  18-23, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 52 \textit{What are the reasons annexed to the second commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:second
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reasons annexed to the second commandment\index{God's law:commandments:second ``f10!} are, God's
sovereignty\index{God's attributes:sovereign lordship ``f10!} over us,\footnote{\ Psalm 95:2-3, 6-7\index{19 Psalms:ch.
95, v.   2-3, 6-7, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 96:9-10\index{19 Psalms:ch.  96, v.   9-10, pg. ``f30!}.} his propriety in
us\index{Providence:God's propriety over mankind ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 19:5\index{02 Exodus:ch.  19, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 45:11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  45, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 54:5\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  54, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}.} and the zeal he\index{Worship:God's zeal for proper ``f10!} has to his own worship\index{Worship:of God
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 34:1\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{02 Exodus:ch.  34, v.  14, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:22\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 53 \textit{Which is the third commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The third commandment\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!} is, You shalt not take the name of the Lord thy God
in vain\index{God's name:not to be:taken in vain ``f10!}; for the Lord will not hold him guiltless\index{God's name:not
guiltless if take in vain ``f10!} that takes his name in vain.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:7\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   7,
pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:11\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 54 \textit{What is required in the third commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The third commandment\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!} requires the holy\index{God's name:holy ``f10!} and
reverend\index{God's name:to be used:reverently in thoughts and words ``f10!} use of God's names, titles\index{God's
name:titles to be honoured ``f10!},\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 10:20\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  10, v.  20, pg. ``f30!};
Psalm 29:2\index{19 Psalms:ch.  29, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 6:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}
attributes\index{God's attributes:to be:revered ``f10!},\footnote{\ 1 Chronicles 29:10-13\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch. 
29, v.  10-13, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 15:3-4\index{66 Revelation:ch.  15, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.}
ordinances,\footnote{\ Acts 2:42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  42, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}.} Word,\footnote{\ Psalm 138:2\index{19 Psalms:ch. 138, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}; Revelation 22:18-19\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}.} and works\index{Providence:God's
works ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 107:21-22\index{19 Psalms:ch. 107, v.  21-22, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 4:11\index{66
Revelation:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 55 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the third
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The third commandment\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!} forbids all profaning or\index{God's name:not to
be:profaned ``f10!} abusing\index{God's name:not to be:abused ``f10!} of anything whereby God makes himself
known.\footnote{\ Leviticus 19:12\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:33-37\index{40 Matthew:ch.
5, v.  33-37, pg. ``f30!}; James 5:12\index{59 James:ch.   5, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 56 \textit{What is }the\textit{ reason annexed to the third commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:third
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reason annexed to the third commandment\index{God's law:commandments:third ``f10!} is, that however the breakers
of this commandment may escape punishment from\index{Punishment:escape from man's ``f10!} men, yet the Lord our God
will not suffer them to escape\index{Punishment:no escape ``f10!} his righteous judgment\index{Judgement:righteous
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 28:58\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.  28, v.  58, pg. ``f30!}{}-59\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch. 
28, v.  58-59, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 3:13\index{09 1 Samuel:ch.   3, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Samuel 4:11\index{09 1
Samuel:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 57 \textit{Which is the }fourth\textit{ commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} is, Remember\index{Sabbath:to be:remembered
``f10!} the sabbath day, to keep it holy\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!}. Six\index{Sabbath:six days:for labour
``f10!} days shalt you labor, and do\index{Sabbath:labour six days, rest on Sabbath ``f10!} all thy work; but the
seven\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}th day is the sabbath of\index{Sabbath:instituted by God ``f10!} the
Lord thy God: in it you shalt not do any work, thou, nor thy son, nor thy daughter, thy manservant, nor thy
maidservant\index{Sabbath:servants not to be made to work ``f10!}, nor thy cattle, nor thy stranger that is within thy
gates. For in six\index{Creation:in six days ``f10!} days the Lord made heaven\index{God's attributes:creator:of heaven
and earth ``f10!} and earth, the sea\index{God's attributes:creator:of sea ``f10!}, and all that in them is, and rested
the\index{Sabbath:God rested the seventh day ``f10!} seventh day\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!}: wherefore the Lord
blessed the\index{Sabbath:blessed ``f10!} sabbath day, and hallowed\index{God's name:hallowed ``f10!}
it.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8-11, pg.
``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:12-15\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  12-15, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 58 \textit{What is required in the fourth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} requires the keeping holy\index{Sabbath:to be:kept
holy ``f10!} to God such set times as he has appointed in his Word\index{Scripture:word of God:standard:for worship
``f10!}; expressly one\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!} whole day in seven, to be a holy sabbath to
himself.\footnote{\ Exodus 31:13, 16-17\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  13, 16-17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 59 \textit{Which day of the seven}\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}\textit{ has God appointed to be the
weekly}\index{Sabbath:weekly ``f10!}\textit{ sabbath?}

A. From the beginning of the world to the resurrection of Christ\index{Jesus:resurrection:from the dead ``f10!}, God
appointed the seven\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}th day of the week to be the
weekly\index{Sabbath:weekly ``f10!} sabbath;\footnote{\ Genesis 2:2-3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!};
Exodus 20:11\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.} and the first day\index{Sabbath:first day of week ``f10!}
of the week ever since, to continue to the end of the world, which is the Christian sabbath.\footnote{\ Mark
2:27-28\index{41 Mark:ch.   2, v.  27-28, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:7\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Corinthians 16:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 1:10\index{66 Revelation:ch.   1, v. 
10, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 60 \textit{How is the sabbath to}\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!}\textit{ be
sanctified}\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sabbath is to\index{Sabbath:to be:kept holy ``f10!} be sanctified\index{Sanctification:sanctification ``f10!} by
a holy resting all that day, even from such worldly employments and recreations\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly employments
and recreations ``f10!} as are lawful on other\index{Sabbath:cease:activities lawful on other days ``f10!}
days;\footnote{\ Exodus 20:10\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Nehemiah 13:15-22\index{16 Nehemiah:ch. 
13, v.  15-22, pg. ``f30!}; Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v. 
13-14, pg. ``f30!}.} and spending\index{Sabbath:spend bulk of time in public and private worship ``f10!} the whole time
in the public and private exercises\index{Worship:private exercises ``f10!} of God's worship\index{Worship:of God
``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:8\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 23:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch. 
23, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 4:16\index{42 Luke:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:7\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.   7,
pg. ``f30!}.} except so much as is to be taken up in the works of necessity and\index{Sabbath:works of necessity and
mercy ``f10!} mercy.\footnote{\ Matthew 12:1-13\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.   1-13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 61 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the fourth
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} forbids the omission\index{Sin:omission of duties
``f10!} or careless performance of the duties required\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}, and
the profaning the\index{Sabbath:not to be profaned ``f10!} day by idleness\index{idleness ``f10!}, or doing that which
is in itself sinful, or by unnecessary thoughts\index{Sabbath:avoid unnecessary, worldly thoughts ``f10!}, words, or
works, about\index{Sabbath:cease:own works ``f10!} our worldly employments or recreations\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly
employments and recreations ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Nehemiah 13:15-22\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.  13, v.  15-22, pg. ``f30!};
Isaiah 58:13\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}{}-14\index{23 Isaiah:ch.  58, v.  13-14, pg. ``f30!}; Amos
8:4-6\index{30 Amos:ch.   8, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 62 \textit{What are the reasons annexed to the fourth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fourth
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reasons annexed to the fourth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fourth ``f10!} are, God's allowing us
six\index{Sabbath:six days:for own affairs ``f10!} days of the week for our own employments\index{Sabbath:cease:worldly
employments and recreations ``f10!},\footnote{\ Exodus 20:9\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus
31:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Leviticus 23:3\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  23, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}.}
his challenging a special propriety in the\index{Sabbath:God's propriety over ``f10!} seventh,
his\index{Sabbath:seventh day ``f10!} own example, and his blessing the sabbath day\index{Sabbath:blessed
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 2:2-3\index{01 Genesis:ch.   2, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 20:11\index{02 Exodus:ch. 
20, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; Exodus 31:17\index{02 Exodus:ch.  31, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 63 \textit{Which is the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!} is, Honour\index{Parents:to be honoured ``f10!} thy
father and thy mother\index{Superiors:styled as fathers and mothers ``f10!}; that thy days may be long upon the land
which the Lord thy God gives you.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:12\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy
5:16\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 64 \textit{What is required in the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!} requires the preserving\index{Equals:preserve honour
of others ``f10!} the honor, and\index{Love for others:seek neighbours' honour ``f10!} performing the
duties\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!}, belonging to everyone in their several places and
relations, as superiors\index{Superiors:styled as fathers and mothers ``f10!}, inferiors, or equals\index{Equals:duties
of ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 13:1\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 7\index{45 Romans:ch.  13, v.   1, 7,
pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}1\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}{}-22, 24\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.  21-22, 24, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:1, 4-5, 9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.  
6, v.   1, 4-5, 9, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:17\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 65 \textit{What is }forbidden\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the fifth
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!} forbids the neglecting of\index{Love for
others:mutual:honour ``f10!}, or doing anything against, the honor and\index{Love for others:advancement of others
``f10!} duty which belongs\index{God's law:commandments:duties:to others ``f10!} to everyone in their several places
and relations.\footnote{\ Matthew 15:4-6\index{40 Matthew:ch.  15, v.   4-6, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 13:8\index{45
Romans:ch.  13, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 66 \textit{What is the }reason\textit{ annexed to the fifth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:fifth
``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The reason annexed to the fifth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:fifth ``f10!} is, a promise of
long\index{God's law:commandments:promises included ``f10!} life and prosperity (as far as it shall serve for God's
glory\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:for God's glory ``f10!} and their own good) to all such as keep this
commandment.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:12\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:16\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 6:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}{}-3\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   6, v.   2-3, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 67 \textit{Which is the sixth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sixth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!} is, You shalt not kill\index{murder, unjust killing
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:13\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:17\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 68 \textit{What is required in the sixth commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sixth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!} requires all lawful endeavors\index{Human
life:protect with:lawful endeavors ``f10!} to preserve our\index{Human life:preservation ``f10!} own life, and the life
of others.\footnote{\ Ephesians 5:2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}8-29\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v. 
28-29, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 69 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the sixth
commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sixth commandment\index{God's law:commandments:sixth ``f10!} forbids the taking away of our own life, or the life
of our neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}, unjustly, or whatsoever tends\index{Human life:defend
``f10!} thereunto.\footnote{\ Genesis 9:6\index{01 Genesis:ch.   9, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 5:22\index{40
Matthew:ch.   5, v.  22, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:1\index{62 1 John:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{62 1 John:ch.   3,
v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 70 \textit{Which }is\textit{ the seven}\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}\textit{th commandment?}

A. The seventh commandment\index{God's law:commandments:seventh ``f10!} is, You shalt not commit adultery\index{Sexual
immorality:adultery ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:14\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy
5:18\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 71 \textit{What is required in the seven}\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}\textit{th commandment?}

A. The seventh commandment\index{God's law:commandments:seventh ``f10!} requires the preservation of our\index{Sexual
purity:preservation ``f10!} own and our neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}{}'s
chastity\index{Chastity:heart, speech, behaviour ``f10!}, in heart\index{Love for others:from heart ``f10!}, speech,
and behavior\index{Good works:behavior ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 7:2-3, 5\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  
2-3, 5, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 4:3-5\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   4, v.   3-5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 72 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the
seven}\index{Sabbath:one whole day in seven ``f10!}\textit{th commandment?}

A. The seventh commandment\index{God's law:commandments:seventh ``f10!} forbids all unchaste\index{Sexual
immorality:unchaste company and thoughts ``f10!} thoughts, words, and actions.\footnote{\ Matthew 5:28\index{40
Matthew:ch.   5, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 5:3-4\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 73 \textit{Which is the eighth}\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The eighth\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!} commandment is, You shalt not steal\index{Theft:stealing
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:15\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:19\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 74 \textit{What is required in the eighth}\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The eighth\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!} commandment requires the lawful procuring\index{Material
things:to be lawfully procured ``f10!} and furthering\index{Love for others:advancement of others ``f10!} the wealth
and outward estate of ourselves and others.\footnote{\ Leviticus 25:35\index{03 Leviticus:ch.  25, v.  35, pg. ``f30!};
Ephesians 4:28\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}b\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28b, pg. ``f30!};
Philippians 2:4\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 75 \textit{What }is\textit{ forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the
eighth}\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The eighth\index{God's law:commandments:eighth ``f10!} commandment forbids whatsoever does, or may, unjustly hinder
our\index{Love for others:advancement of others ``f10!} own, or our neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self
``f10!}{}'s, wealth or outward estate.\footnote{\ Proverbs 28:19\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}ff,
Ephesians 4:28\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28, pg. ``f30!}a\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  28a, pg. ``f30!}; 1
Thessalonians 3:10\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 5:8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   5, v. 
8, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 76 \textit{Which is the ninth}\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The ninth\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!} commandment is, You shalt not bear false witness
against\index{Falsehood:false witness against neighbour ``f10!} thy neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:16\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:20\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 77 \textit{What is required in the ninth}\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The ninth\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!} commandment requires the maintaining and
promoting\index{Truth:maintain and promote ``f10!} of truth between man and man, and of our own and our
neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}{}'s good name,\footnote{\ Zechariah 8:16\index{38
Zechariah:ch.   8, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 25:10\index{44 Acts:ch.  25, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; 3 John 12\index{64 3
John:v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} especially in witness bearing\index{Truth:in witness bearing ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Proverbs
14:5, 25\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  14, v.   5, 25, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 78 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the ninth}\index{God's
law:commandments:ninth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The ninth\index{God's law:commandments:ninth ``f10!} commandment forbids whatsoever is
prejudicial\index{Falsehood:prejudicing truth or justice ``f10!} to truth, or injurious to our own, or our
neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}{}'s, good name.\footnote{\ Leviticus 19:16\index{03
Leviticus:ch.  19, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 15:3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  15, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Proverbs
6:16-19\index{20 Proverbs:ch.   6, v.  16-19, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 3:14\index{42 Luke:ch.   3, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 79 \textit{Which is the tenth}\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The tenth\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!} commandment is, You shalt not
covet\index{Covetousness:covetousness ``f10!} thy neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}{}'s house,
you\index{Covetousness:nothing of neighbour ``f10!} shalt not covet thy neighbour's wife, nor his manservant, nor his
maidservant\index{Sabbath:servants not to be made to work ``f10!}, nor his ox, nor his ass, nor anything that is thy
neighbour's.\footnote{\ Exodus 20:17\index{02 Exodus:ch.  20, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Deuteronomy 5:21\index{05
Deuteronomy:ch.   5, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 80 \textit{What is required in the tenth}\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The tenth\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!} commandment requires full contentment\index{contentment ``f10!}
with our own condition,\footnote{\ Psalm 34:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  34, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 4:11\index{50
Philippians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews
13:5\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  13, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.} with a right and charitable\index{Love for others:charitable
thoughts ``f10!} frame of spirit toward our neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}, and all that is
his.\footnote{\ Luke 15:6, 9, 11-32\index{42 Luke:ch.  15, v.   6, 9, 11-32, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 12:15\index{45
Romans:ch.  12, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 2:4\index{50 Philippians:ch.   2, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip

Q. 81 \textit{What is forbidden}\index{God's law:commandments:sins forbidden ``f10!}\textit{ in the tenth}\index{God's
law:commandments:tenth ``f10!}\textit{ commandment?}

A. The tenth\index{God's law:commandments:tenth ``f10!} commandment forbids all discontentment\index{discontentment
``f10!} with our own estate,\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 10:10\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; James
3:1\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4-16\index{59 James:ch.   3, v.  14-16, pg. ``f30!}.}
envying\index{Envy:envy ``f10!} or grieving at\index{Envy:grieving at success of others ``f10!} the good of our
neighbour\index{Love for others:neighbour as self ``f10!}, and all inordinate motions\index{Covetousness:inordinate
affections to others' goods ``f10!} and affections to anything that is his.\footnote{\ Galatians 5:2\index{48
Galatians:ch.   5, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}6\index{48 Galatians:ch.   5, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:5\index{51
Colossians:ch.   3, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 82 \textit{Is any man able perfectly to keep the commandment}\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam
``f10!}\textit{s}\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!}\textit{ of God?}

A. No mere man, since the fall\index{Sin:original:first transgression (of Adam) ``f10!}, is able in this life perfectly
to keep the commandment\index{God's law:commandments:given to Adam ``f10!}s\index{God's law:commandments:ten ``f10!} of
God, but does daily break the\index{Lord's Supper:bread broken ``f10!}m\index{God's law:broken daily by all men
(thought, word, deed) ``f10!} in thought, word, and deed.\footnote{\ Genesis 8:21\index{01 Genesis:ch.   8, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}; Romans 3:9\index{45 Romans:ch.   3, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}ff, 23.}


\bigskip

Q. 83 \textit{Are all transgressions}\index{God's law:commandments:transgressions ``f10!}\textit{ of the law equally
heinous}\index{God's law:commandments:all transgression equally heinous ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Some sins in themselves, and by reason of several aggravations\index{Sin:aggravations:which compound ``f10!}, are
more heinous\index{Sin:aggravations:make more heinous ``f10!} in the sight of God than others.\footnote{\ Ezekiel 8:6,
13, 15\index{26 Ezekiel:ch.   8, v.   6, 13, 15, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 11:20-24\index{40 Matthew:ch.  11, v.  20-24, pg.
``f30!}; John 19:11\index{43 John:ch.  19, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 84 \textit{What does every sin deserve}\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Every sin deserves\index{Sin:deserves damnation ``f10!} God's wrath and\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!}
curse,\index{Curse:of God ``f10!} both in this life, and that which is to come.\footnote{\ Matthew 25:41\index{40
Matthew:ch.  25, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:10\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians
5:6\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   5, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}; James 2:10\index{59 James:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 85 \textit{What does God require of us}\index{God's law:commandments:duties:required by God ``f10!}\textit{, that we
may escape}\index{Wrath:of God:requirements to escape ``f10!}\textit{ his wrath and}\index{Wrath:of God:for sin
``f10!}\textit{ curse,}\index{Curse:of God ``f10!}\textit{ due to us for sin?}

A. To escape\index{Wrath:of God:requirements to escape ``f10!} the wrath and\index{Wrath:of God:for sin ``f10!} curse of
God\index{Curse:of God ``f10!}, due to us for sin, God requires of us\index{Repentance:required for pardon ``f10!}
faith in Jesus\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!} Christ, repentance unto\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!}
life,\footnote{\ Mark 1:15\index{41 Mark:ch.   1, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:21\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  21, pg.
``f30!}.} with the diligent use\index{Grace:diligent use of means ``f10!} of all the outward means whereby Christ
communicates to us the benefits of redemption\index{Believers:benefits:of redemption ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Acts
2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}4\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24, pg. ``f30!}{}-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  24-25, pg.
``f30!}; Colossians 3:16\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 86 \textit{What is faith in Jesus}\index{Faith:in Jesus Christ ``f10!}\textit{ Christ?}

A. Faith\index{Faith:saving ``f10!} in Jesus Christ is a saving grace\index{Grace:of salvation
``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 2:8\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   2, v.  
8-9, pg. ``f30!}; cf. Romans 4:16\index{45 Romans:ch.   4, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby we receive and rest upon him
alone for salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, as he is offered to us\index{Faith:receives Jesus
as offered in Gospel ``f10!} in the gospel\index{Gospel:gospel ``f10!}.\footnote{\ John 20:30-31\index{43 John:ch.  20,
v.  30-31, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 2:15-16\index{48 Galatians:ch.   2, v.  15-16, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians
3:3-11\index{50 Philippians:ch.   3, v.   3-11, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 87 \textit{What is repentance unto}\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!}\textit{ life?}

A. Repentance\index{Repentance:unto life ``f10!} unto life is a saving grace\index{Grace:of salvation
``f10!},\footnote{\ Acts 11:18\index{44 Acts:ch.  11, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 2:2\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.
2, pg. ``f30!}5\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   2, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}.} whereby a sinner, out of a true sense of his sin,
and apprehension\index{Repentance:apprehension of God's mercy ``f10!} of the mercy of\index{God's attributes:merciful
``f10!} God in Christ,\footnote{\ Psalm 51:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-4\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51,
v.   1-4, pg. ``f30!}; Joel 2:13\index{29 Joel:ch.   2, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 15:7, 10\index{42 Luke:ch.  15, v.  
7, 10, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:37\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  37, pg. ``f30!}.} does, with grief\index{Sin:grief and hatred
of ``f10!} and hatred of his\index{Sin:to be hated ``f10!} sin, turn from it unto God,\footnote{\ Jeremiah
31:18\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{24 Jeremiah:ch.  31, v.  18-19, pg. ``f30!}; Luke
1:16-17\index{42 Luke:ch.   1, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Thessalonians 1:9\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   1, v.   9,
pg. ``f30!}.} with full purpose of, and endeavour after\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:endeavoring ``f10!}, new
obedience\index{Believers:obedience:strive for new ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 2 Chronicles 7:14\index{14 2 Chronicles:ch.   7,
v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 119:5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}7-64\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.  57-64,
pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 3:8\index{40 Matthew:ch.   3, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 7:1\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.  
7, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}0\index{47 2 Corinthians:ch.   7, v.  10, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 88 \textit{What are the outward and ordinary means whereby Christ communicates to us the }benefits\textit{ of
redemption}\index{Believers:benefits:of redemption ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The outward and ordinary means whereby Christ communicates to us the benefits of
redemption\index{Believers:benefits:of redemption ``f10!} are, his ordinances, especially\index{Church:furnished
with:ordinances of God ``f10!} the Word, sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, and prayer;
all\index{Prayer:act of worship ``f10!} which are made effectual\index{Worship:ordinances:made effectual for salvation
``f10!} to the elect\index{Election:elect of God ``f10!} for salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 28:18\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v. 
18-20, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 2:41\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}{}-42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  41-42, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 89 \textit{How is the Word made effectual}\index{Scripture:word of God:for salvation ``f10!}\textit{ to
salvation}\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The Spirit\index{Holy Spirit:Holy Spirit ``f10!} of God makes the reading\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard
``f10!}, but especially the preaching of the Word\index{Preaching:ministry of the Word ``f10!}, an
effectual\index{Preaching:effectual means of convincing and enlightening ``f10!} means of convincing
and\index{Preaching:convincing and converting sinners ``f10!} converting\index{Conversion:conversion ``f10!} sinners,
and of building them\index{Holy Spirit:builds up the elect ``f10!} up in holiness and\index{Believers:holy:being
perfected ``f10!} comfort, through\index{Faith:source of comfort ``f10!} faith, unto salvation\index{Salvation:belief
in Jesus by faith ``f10!} [a].\footnote{\ Nehemiah 8:8\index{16 Nehemiah:ch.   8, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}{}-9\index{16
Nehemiah:ch.   8, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 20:32\index{44 Acts:ch.  20, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 10:1\index{45
Romans:ch.  10, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{45 Romans:ch.  10, v. 
14-17, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Timothy 3:15\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{55 2 Timothy:ch.   3, v. 
15-17, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 90 \textit{How is the Word }to\textit{ be read}\index{Scripture:to be:read and heard ``f10!}\textit{ and heard, that
it may become effectual}\index{Sacraments:effectual means of salvation ``f10!}\textit{ to
salvation}\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. That the Word may\index{Scripture:word of God:for salvation ``f10!} become effectual\index{Sacraments:effectual means
of salvation ``f10!} to salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, we must attend thereunto with
diligence\index{Preaching:diligence in application ``f10!}, preparation, and\index{Preaching:preparation for ``f10!}
prayer;\footnote{\ Deuteronomy 6:6\index{05 Deuteronomy:ch.   6, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}ff, Psalm 119:18\index{19
Psalms:ch. 119, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 2:1-2\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg. ``f30!}.} receive it with
faith\index{Faith:in prayer ``f10!} and love, lay\index{Scripture:lay up in heart ``f10!} it up in our
hearts\index{Heart:new:through ministry of Word ``f10!}, and practice it in our lives.\footnote{\ Psalm 119:11\index{19
Psalms:ch. 119, v.  11, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 2:10\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   2, v.  10, pg. ``f30!};
Hebrews 4:2\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   4, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}; James 1:22\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  22, pg.
``f30!}{}-25\index{59 James:ch.   1, v.  22-25, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 91 \textit{How do the sacraments}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ become
effectual}\index{Sacraments:effectual means of salvation ``f10!}\textit{ means of salvation}\index{Salvation:belief in
Jesus by faith ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} become effectual\index{Sacraments:effectual means of
salvation ``f10!} means of salvation\index{Salvation:belief in Jesus by faith ``f10!}, not from any
virtue\index{Sacraments:grace:not conferred by elements ``f10!} in them, or in him that does administer them; but only
by the blessing of Christ, and the working of his\index{Salvation:by working of Holy Spirit ``f10!} Spirit in them that
by faith\index{Faith:worked in believers by the Holy Spirit ``f10!} receive them.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 3:7\index{46
1 Corinthians:ch.   3, v.   7, pg. ``f30!} cf. 1 Corinthians 1:12-17\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  12-17, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 92 \textit{What is a sacrament}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. A sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} is an holy ordinance instituted by
Christ\index{Sacraments:instituted by:Christ ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}; Matthew 26:26\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  26, v.  26-28, pg.
``f30!}; Mark 14:22-25\index{41 Mark:ch.  14, v.  22-25, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 22:19\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19, pg.
``f30!}{}-20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 1:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.   2,
pg. ``f30!}2-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.   1, v.  22-26, pg. ``f30!}.} wherein, by sensible
signs\index{Sacraments:holy:signs ``f10!}, Christ, and the benefits of the\index{Covenant:grace:benefits ``f10!} new
covenant, are\index{Covenant:new:benefits ``f10!} represented\index{Sacraments:represent Christ ``f10!}, sealed,
and\index{Sacraments:benefits:sealed ``f10!} applied to believers\index{Sacraments:applied to believers
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Galatians 3:27\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  27, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1
Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16-17, pg. ``f30!}.}

Q. 93 \textit{Which are the sacraments}\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}\textit{ of the New
Testament}\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The sacraments\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!} of the New Testament\index{Scripture:New Testament ``f10!}
are, Baptism\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.}
and the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch. 
11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v. 
23-26, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 94 \textit{What is Baptism}\index{Baptism:definition ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Baptism is a\index{Baptism:sacrament ``f10!} sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!}, wherein the
washing\index{Baptism:washing with water ``f10!} with water in\index{Baptism:to use water ``f10!} the name of the
Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!}, and of the Son\index{Jesus:Son of God ``f10!}, and of the Holy Ghost\index{Holy
Spirit:Holy Ghost ``f10!},\footnote{\ Matthew 28:19\index{40 Matthew:ch.  28, v.  19, pg. ``f30!}.} does
signify\index{Baptism:sign of ingrafting into Christ ``f10!} and seal our\index{Baptism:seal of salvation ``f10!}
ingrafting\index{Believers:ingrafted into Christ ``f10!} into Christ, and partaking of the benefits of
the\index{Covenant:grace:benefits ``f10!} covenant of grace\index{Covenant:grace:grace ``f10!}, and our engagement to
be\index{Oaths and Vows:engagements to God ``f10!} the Lord's.\footnote{\ Acts 2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg.
``f30!}{}-42\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38-42, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 22:16\index{44 Acts:ch.  22, v.  16, pg. ``f30!};
Romans 6:3-4\index{45 Romans:ch.   6, v.   3-4, pg. ``f30!}; Galatians 3:26-27\index{48 Galatians:ch.   3, v.  26-27,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Peter 3:21\index{60 1 Peter:ch.   3, v.  21, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 95 \textit{To whom is Baptism to be administered}\index{Baptism:recipients ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Baptism is not to be administered to any\index{Baptism:not to be administered outside those in visible church ``f10!}
that are out of the visible church\index{Church:visible ``f10!}, till they profess their faith\index{Faith:profession
of ``f10!} in Christ, and obedience\index{God's law:commandments:obedience:required ``f10!} to him;\footnote{\ Acts.
2:41; Acts 8:12, 36\index{44 Acts:ch.   8, v.  12, 36, pg. ``f30!}, 38\index{44 Acts:ch.   8, v.  12, 36, 38, pg.
``f30!}; Acts 18:8\index{44 Acts:ch.  18, v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} but the infants of such\index{Infants:of believing
parents, to be baptized ``f10!} as are members of the\index{Church members ``f10!} visible church are to be
baptized\index{Baptism:infants ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Genesis 17:7\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, pg. ``f30!},
9\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 9, pg. ``f30!}{}-11\index{01 Genesis:ch.  17, v.   7, 9-11, pg. ``f30!}; Acts
2:38\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38, pg. ``f30!}{}-39\index{44 Acts:ch.   2, v.  38-39, pg. ``f30!}; Acts 16:32\index{44
Acts:ch.  16, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}{}-33\index{44 Acts:ch.  16, v.  32-33, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 2:11-12\index{51
Colossians:ch.   2, v.  11-12, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 96 \textit{What is }the\textit{ Lord's Supper}\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. The Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!} is a sacrament\index{Sacraments:holy:ordinances ``f10!},
wherein, by giving and receiving\index{Lord's Supper:defined ``f10!} bread and\index{Lord's Supper:bread ``f10!}
wine\index{Lord's Supper:wine ``f10!}, according to Christ's appointment\index{Lord's Supper:proper administration
``f10!}, his death\index{Jesus:death:death ``f10!} is showed forth;\footnote{\ Luke 22:19\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v. 
19, pg. ``f30!}{}-20\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  19-20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11,
v.   2, pg. ``f30!}3\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-26\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v. 
23-26, pg. ``f30!}.} and the worthy\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!} receivers are, not
after a corporal\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:not corporal ``f10!} and carnal manner\index{Lord's
Supper:spiritual feeding:not carnal ``f10!}, but by faith, made partakers of his\index{Lord's Supper:partakers of
Christ through faith ``f10!} body and blood\index{Lord's Supper:body and blood of Jesus ``f10!}, with all his benefits,
to\index{Lord's Supper:benefits believers receive ``f10!} their spiritual nourishment\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual
feeding:nourishment ``f10!}, and growth in grace\index{Sanctification:spiritual growth:in grace ``f10!}.\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 10:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16, pg. ``f30!}{}-17\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  16-17,
pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 97 \textit{What is required for the worthy}\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!}\textit{
receiving of the}\index{Worship:administration of sacraments ``f10!}\textit{ Lord's Supper}\index{Lord's
Supper:sacrament ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. It is required of them that would worthily\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual feeding:worthy receivers ``f10!} partake of
the Lord's Supper\index{Lord's Supper:sacrament ``f10!}, that they examine themselves\index{Lord's
Supper:preparation:self-examination ``f10!} of their knowledge to discern the\index{Lord's Supper:discern Lord's body
``f10!} Lord's body, of their faith to\index{Faith:applied in Lord's Supper ``f10!} feed\index{Lord's Supper:spiritual
feeding:in faith ``f10!} upon him, of their repentance\index{Repentance:for all sins ``f10!}, love, and new
obedience\index{Believers:obedience:strive for new ``f10!}; lest, coming unworthily\index{Lord's Supper:unworthy
participation ``f10!}, they eat and drink judgment to\index{Judgement:temporal ``f10!} themselves.\footnote{\ 1
Corinthians 11:2\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}7\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27, pg.
``f30!}{}-32\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  11, v.  27-32, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip


\bigskip


Q. 98 \textit{What is prayer}\index{Prayer:defined ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. Prayer is an\index{Prayer:defined ``f10!} offering up of our\index{Prayer:offering desires to God ``f10!} desires
unto God,\footnote{\ Psalm 10:17\index{19 Psalms:ch.  10, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 62:8\index{19 Psalms:ch.  62, v.  
8, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 7:7-8\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   7-8, pg. ``f30!}.} for things
agreeable\index{Prayer:requests agreeable to God's will ``f10!} to his will,\footnote{\ 1 John 5:14\index{62 1 John:ch.
5, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} in the name of Christ,\footnote{\ John 16:2\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.   2, pg.
``f30!}3\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}{}-24\index{43 John:ch.  16, v.  23-24, pg. ``f30!}.} with
confession\index{Confession:of sin ``f10!} of our sins,\footnote{\ Psalm 32:5\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5, pg.
``f30!}{}-6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  32, v.   5-6, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 9:4\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4, pg.
``f30!}{}-19\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4-19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:9\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}.}
and thankful\index{Prayer:thanking God ``f10!} acknowledgement\index{Judgement day:believers:acknowledged by God
``f10!} of his mercies\index{God's attributes:merciful ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 103:1\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.   1,
pg. ``f30!}{}-5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.   1-5, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 136; Philippians 4:6\index{50 Philippians:ch.  
4, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 99 \textit{What rule has God given for}\index{Prayer:direction for ``f10!}\textit{ our direction in prayer?}

A. The whole Word of God\index{Scripture:word of God:word of God ``f10!} is of use to direct us in
prayer\index{Prayer:direction for ``f10!};\footnote{\ 1 John 5:14\index{62 1 John:ch.   5, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.} but
the special rule of direction is that form of prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:pattern for our prayers ``f10!} which Christ
taught his\index{Prayer:Lord's:Jesus taught his disciples ``f10!} disciples\index{disciples of Jesus ``f10!}, commonly
called The Lord's Prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:The Lord's Prayer ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Matthew 6:9\index{40 Matthew:ch.  
6, v.   9, pg. ``f30!}{}-13\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.   9-13, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 100 \textit{What does the preface of}\index{Prayer:Lord's:preface ``f10!}\textit{ }the\textit{ Lord's
Prayer}\index{Prayer:Lord's:The Lord's Prayer ``f10!}\textit{ teach us?}

A. The preface of\index{Prayer:Lord's:preface ``f10!} the Lord's Prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:The Lord's Prayer ``f10!},
which is, Our Father\index{Father:God the ``f10!} which art in heaven\index{Heaven:God's abode ``f10!}, teaches us to
draw near\index{Prayer:draw near to God ``f10!} to God with all holy\index{Prayer:holy reverence ``f10!}
reverence\footnote{\ Psalm 95:6\index{19 Psalms:ch.  95, v.   6, pg. ``f30!}.} and confidence\index{Prayer:with
confidence ``f10!},\footnote{\ Ephesians 3:12\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  12, pg. ``f30!}.} as children to a
father,\footnote{\ Matthew 7:9-11\index{40 Matthew:ch.   7, v.   9-11, pg. ``f30!}; cf. Luke 11:11-13\index{42 Luke:ch.
11, v.  11-13, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 8:1\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}5\index{45 Romans:ch.   8, v.  15,
pg. ``f30!}.} able and ready to help\index{Prayer:helped by Holy Spirit ``f10!} us;\footnote{\ Ephesians 3:20\index{49
Ephesians:ch.   3, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.} and that we should pray with an\index{Prayer:praising God
``f10!}d\index{Prayer:for others ``f10!} for others.\footnote{\ Ephesians 6:18\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   6, v.  18, pg.
``f30!}; 1 Timothy 2:1\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   2, v.   1-2, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 101 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the first
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:first ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the first petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:first ``f10!}, which is, Hallowed\index{God's name:hallowed
``f10!} be thy name, we pray, that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} God would
enable\index{Worship:correct:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} us, and others, to glorify\index{Worship:glorifying God
``f10!} him in all that whereby he makes himself known;\footnote{\ Psalm 67:1-3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  67, v.   1-3, pg.
``f30!}; Psalm 99:3\index{19 Psalms:ch.  99, v.   3, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm 100:3-4\index{19 Psalms:ch. 100, v.   3-4, pg.
``f30!}.} and that he would dispose all\index{Providence:God disposes all things for his glory ``f10!} things to his
own glory\index{God's attributes:glory:his own ``f10!}.\footnote{\ Romans 11:33\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33, pg.
``f30!}{}-36\index{45 Romans:ch.  11, v.  33-36, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 4:11\index{66 Revelation:ch.   4, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 102 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the second
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:second ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the second petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:second ``f10!}, which is, Thy kingdom come\index{Kingdom of
God:prayer for advancement ``f10!}, we pray, that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} Satan's
kingdom may be destroyed\index{Prayer:for kingdom of sin to be destroyed ``f10!};\footnote{\ Matthew 12:25\index{40
Matthew:ch.  12, v.  25, pg. ``f30!}{}-28\index{40 Matthew:ch.  12, v.  25-28, pg. ``f30!}; Romans 16:2\index{45
Romans:ch.  16, v.   2, pg. ``f30!}0\index{45 Romans:ch.  16, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 3:8\index{62 1 John:ch.   3,
v.   8, pg. ``f30!}.} and that the kingdom of grace may be\index{Grace:kingdom of (advanced) ``f10!}
advanced,\footnote{\ Psalm 72:8-11\index{19 Psalms:ch.  72, v.   8-11, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 24:14\index{40 Matthew:ch. 
24, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 15:24-25\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  15, v.  24-25, pg. ``f30!}.} ourselves and
others brought into it, and kept in it;\footnote{\ Psalm 119:5\index{19 Psalms:ch. 119, v.   5, pg. ``f30!}; Luke
22:32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Thessalonians 3:1\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   1, pg.
``f30!}{}-5\index{53 2 Thessalonians:ch.   3, v.   1-5, pg. ``f30!}.} and that the kingdom of glory
may\index{Prayer:for glory of God ``f10!} be hastened\index{Kingdom:of glory, desire to see hastened
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Revelation 22:20\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 103 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the third
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:third ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the third petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:third ``f10!}, which is, Thy will be done in earth, as it is in
heaven\index{Heaven:God's will done ``f10!}, we pray, that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} God,
by his grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!}, would make us able and willing to know\index{Conversion:renewal of the
will ``f10!}, obey, and\index{God's law:obligation to obey:in all things ``f10!} submit\index{Holy Spirit:subdues will
of man ``f10!} to his will in all things,\footnote{\ Psalm 19:14\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}; Psalm
119; 1 Thessalonians 5:23\index{52 1 Thessalonians:ch.   5, v.  23, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 13:20-21\index{58 Hebrews:ch. 
13, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}.} as the angels\index{Angels:angels ``f10!} do in heaven\index{Angels:works in heaven
``f10!}.\footnote{\ Psalm 103:20-21\index{19 Psalms:ch. 103, v.  20-21, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 1:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.  
1, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}4\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   1, v.  14, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 104 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the fourth
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fourth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the fourth petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fourth ``f10!}, which is, Give us this day our daily
bread\index{Prayer:for daily needs ``f10!}, we pray that of God's free gift we\index{Providence:provides good gifts
``f10!} may receive a competent portion\index{Prayer:for necessities ``f10!} of the good things of this life, and enjoy
his blessing with them.\footnote{\ Proverbs 30:8-9\index{20 Proverbs:ch.  30, v.   8-9, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew
6:31-34\index{40 Matthew:ch.   6, v.  31-34, pg. ``f30!}; Philippians 4:11\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.  11, pg.
``f30!}, 19\index{50 Philippians:ch.   4, v.  11, 19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 6:6\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   6,
pg. ``f30!}{}-8\index{54 1 Timothy:ch.   6, v.   6-8, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 105 \textit{What do we pray for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the fifth
petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fifth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the fifth petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:fifth ``f10!}, which is, And forgive us\index{Forgiveness:beg
pardon for ``f10!} our debts\index{Forgiveness:of debtors ``f10!}, as we forgive our debtors, we pray that
God\index{Prayer:for pardon of sin ``f10!}, for Christ's sake, would freely\index{Salvation:freely offered ``f10!}
pardon all our sins;\footnote{\ Psalm 51:1\index{19 Psalms:ch.  51, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}{}-2, 7, 9\index{19 Psalms:ch. 
51, v.   1-2, 7, 9, pg. ``f30!}; Daniel 9:17\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}{}-19\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9,
v.  17-19, pg. ``f30!}; 1 John 1:7\index{62 1 John:ch.   1, v.   7, pg. ``f30!}.} which we are the rather
encouraged\index{Prayer:assurance of being heard ``f10!} to ask, because by his grace\index{Grace:God's free ``f10!} we
are enabled from\index{Forgiveness:enabled by Holy Spirit ``f10!} the heart to forgive others.\footnote{\ Matthew
18:21-35\index{40 Matthew:ch.  18, v.  21-35, pg. ``f30!}; Ephesians 4:3\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.   3, pg.
``f30!}2\index{49 Ephesians:ch.   4, v.  32, pg. ``f30!}; Colossians 3:13\index{51 Colossians:ch.   3, v.  13, pg.
``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 106 \textit{What do we }pray\textit{ for in}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!}\textit{ the
sixth petition}\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:sixth ``f10!}\textit{?}

A. In the sixth petition\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:sixth ``f10!}, which is, And lead us not into
temptation\index{Temptation:temptation ``f10!}, but deliver us from\index{Salvation:delivered from thraldom to sin
``f10!} evil, we pray, that\index{Prayer:Lord's:petitions:items to pray for ``f10!} God would either keep us from being
tempted to sin,\footnote{\ Psalm 19:13\index{19 Psalms:ch.  19, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; Matthew 26:41\index{40 Matthew:ch.
26, v.  41, pg. ``f30!}; John 17:15\index{43 John:ch.  17, v.  15, pg. ``f30!}.} or support and deliver us
when\index{Temptation:delivery from ``f10!} we are tempted.\footnote{\ Luke 22:31-32\index{42 Luke:ch.  22, v.  31-32,
pg. ``f30!}; 1 Corinthians 10:13\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  10, v.  13, pg. ``f30!}; 2 Corinthians 12:7-9\index{47 2
Corinthians:ch.  12, v.   7-9, pg. ``f30!}; Hebrews 2:1\index{58 Hebrews:ch.   2, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}8\index{58
Hebrews:ch.   2, v.  18, pg. ``f30!}.}


\bigskip

Q. 107 \textit{What }does \textit{the conclusion}\index{Prayer:Lord's:conclusion ``f10!}\textit{ of the Lord's
Prayer}\index{Prayer:Lord's:The Lord's Prayer ``f10!}\textit{ teach us?}

A. The conclusion\index{Prayer:Lord's:conclusion ``f10!} of the Lord's Prayer\index{Prayer:Lord's:The Lord's Prayer
``f10!}, which is, For thine is the kingdom, and the\index{Kingdom of God:prayer ascribing power and glory ``f10!}
power, and the glory, for\index{Prayer:for glory of God ``f10!} ever, Amen\index{Amen, testimony of our true desire for
God's glory ``f10!}. teaches us to take our encouragement in\index{Prayer:drawing encouragement ``f10!} prayer from God
only,\footnote{\ Daniel 9:4\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4, pg. ``f30!}, 7-9, 16-19\index{27 Daniel:ch.   9, v.   4,
7-9, 16-19, pg. ``f30!}; Luke 18:1\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.   1, pg. ``f30!}, 7-8\index{42 Luke:ch.  18, v.   1, 7-8,
pg. ``f30!}.} and in our prayers\index{Prayer:praising God ``f10!} to praise him, ascribing kingdom, power, and glory
to him;\footnote{\ 1 Chronicles 29:10-13\index{13 1 Chronicles:ch.  29, v.  10-13, pg. ``f30!}; 1 Timothy 1:17\index{54
1 Timothy:ch.   1, v.  17, pg. ``f30!}; Revelation 5:11-13\index{66 Revelation:ch.   5, v.  11-13, pg. ``f30!}.} and,
in testimony of our desire, and\index{Prayer:offering desires to God ``f10!} assurance to be\index{Prayer:assurance of
being heard ``f10!} heard, we say, Amen.\footnote{\ 1 Corinthians 14:16\index{46 1 Corinthians:ch.  14, v.  16, pg.
``f30!}; Revelation 22:20\index{66 Revelation:ch.  22, v.  20, pg. ``f30!}.}
